Alcazar Castle is Bombed and Destroyed, The Most Tragic Scene in the Spanish Civil War, The Rebel Army is Surrounded and Dies Without Surrendering, Important Strategic Location

Andaya Alcazar Castle, which had been defended by a small number of rebels for seven weeks, was blown up by government troops today with a landmine under the castle, causing the castle to be almost completely destroyed. Before the government troops detonated the landmine, they ordered all the civilians in the town of Toledo to move to a place one and a half miles away from the town at night to avoid being affected. These people all lived in tents in the strong wind (Reuters telegram, 18th).

Andaya A column of rebel troops who went to the rescue fought hard at night, but are still 14 miles away from Alcazar. The famous Moroccan-style castle in the area has been completely destroyed. The 1,000 rebels in the besieged castle, including 600 women and children, are still determined not to surrender and await the arrival of death. The bombing of Alcazar Castle can be regarded as the most tragic scene in the Spanish Civil War. On the rebel side, the fall of this castle has a greater impact than the occupation of Oviedo or Huesca by government troops. From a military perspective, the importance of this castle is because the location of Alcazar can control the avenue to Madrid and the railway from Alicante to Valencia. Whoever can control the Toledo area, the main port will fall into whose hands. This is a major element in the defense of Madrid, because the food in the area is completely imported through this road (Reuters telegram, 18th).

Madrid After the government troops bombed Alcazar Castle at 6:15 AM this morning, they engaged in hand-to-hand combat with the rebels in the tile yard (National Telegram, 17th).

Andaya Since the besieged rebels who defended the historically famous Moroccan-style castle Alcazar of Toledo refused to surrender, the government troops are now continuing their offensive and carrying out landmine work. It is heard that a large number of landmines have been transported to the center of Alcazar through the dug tunnels, and they may be detonated at any time. According to reports from the rebel side, the mountain town of Ronda and the fortress in the Malaga area have been occupied by the revolutionary army, but well-informed sources in La Rina do not believe this news. According to travelers who recently went to Malaga, the city will not fall for a while. The government troops are in a difficult situation due to the lack of bullets and gasoline, but it is heard that a large number of weapons and bullets transported from Mexico will arrive in Malaga today. The rebels also claimed that the revolutionary army killed 3,000 government troops in the Toledo area in the past few days, and claimed that the revolutionary army also won major victories in the Guadarrama and Zimosira areas (Reuters telegram, 18th).

Seville The radio station of the National Army here recently broadcasted a message saying that the National Army launched an attack on the Darafanla front line south of Beijing yesterday, killing more than 1,000 Marxist Party troops. General Asensio, the commander of the government troops there, was almost captured alive. Madrid Cabinet Prime Minister Caballero asked the Barcelona authorities for help because the city of Toledo south of Beijing is a military-industrial production base and is now threatened by the National Army, and requested that they send fresh troops to transport military supplies to Beijing for use. In addition, the Madrid Civil Corps is digging trenches on the streets (Havas telegram, 18th).

Legislative Yuan Passes Shipbuilding Encouragement Statute

Also Passes Jiangxi Land Consolidation Public Bonds Statute

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 72nd meeting on the morning of the 18th. Sixty-five members, including Wu Huanzhang, and the new member Wang Yuxiang attended. After Chairman Ke Ke and Secretary-General Liang Han Cao led the entire assembly in a three-minute silent tribute to commemorate the September 18th National Crisis, they discussed the agenda. (1) The Jiangxi Province Land Consolidation Public Bonds Statute and Repayment Schedule for the 25th year of the Republic [1936] was passed with amendments. (2) The Shipbuilding Encouragement Act was passed with amendments, and the title was changed to Shipbuilding Encouragement Statute. (3) The National Construction Commission's request to reconsider the Statute for Suppressing Electricity Theft was rejected on the grounds that it did not meet the reconsideration procedures. (4) The Baojia Statute was passed with amendments. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

(Nanjing) The Jiangxi Province Land Consolidation Public Bonds Statute, passed by the Legislative Yuan on the 18th, consists of fourteen articles. The total amount of the public bonds is set at 3 million yuan, with an annual interest rate of 6%. The bonds will be issued on October 1st of this year and will be used specifically as collateral for commercial loans. The bond certificates will be in denominations of 100 yuan, 1,000 yuan, and 10,000 yuan and will be unregistered. They will be sold at 98% of their face value. Interest will be paid twice a year, on March 31st and September 30th. The first principal repayment date is set for March 31st of the 27th year of the Republic [1938]. Repayment will be made in five years using a lottery method, with principal repaid once every six months, until September 30th of the 31st year of the Republic [1942], when the principal and interest will be fully repaid. The source of funds for principal and interest repayment will be the income from land registration certificates and mapping across the province, as well as the increased land tax revenue resulting from land consolidation. The collection agencies in each county will collect the funds and remit them on schedule to the fund management committee for deposit in special accounts at the Central Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Jiangxi Yumin Bank for reserve payment. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Key Points of the Shipbuilding Encouragement Statute

(Nanjing) The Shipbuilding Encouragement Statute, passed by the Legislative Yuan on the 18th, consists of seventeen articles. The purpose of the enactment of this statute is twofold: first, to encourage shipbuilding to demonstrate promotion; and second, to strive for control in order to avoid abuses. There are eight key points: (1) Shipyards will not be rewarded; only shipowners will be rewarded. (2) Engines are all purchased from foreign countries and cannot be manufactured domestically for the time being, so they will not be rewarded for now. (3) The ships that currently sail the most along the Yangtze River and the coast generally range from 500 to 3,000 tons, and 80% of them are foreign-flagged. In order to recover rights and interests, it is necessary to actively encourage shipbuilding, so a five-tier reward standard is specifically stipulated: 12 yuan per ton for ships of 500 tons or more but less than 1,000 tons; 16 yuan per ton for ships of 1,000 tons or more but less than 2,000 tons; 20 yuan per ton for ships of 2,000 tons or more but less than 3,000 tons; 24 yuan per ton for ships of 3,000 tons or more but less than 5,000 tons; and 28 yuan per ton for ships of 5,000 tons or more. (4) Ships under 500 tons mostly operate on inland rivers and are less important, so they are not included in the rewards. (5) Ships are of great importance to military transport, so the statute specifies that the Ministry of Navy should be consulted for review and approval. (6) Because higher speeds require greater effort and expense, which is not economical, and because the wharves along the Yangtze River and the coast are often very narrow and subject to tidal restrictions, speed will not be rewarded for the time being. (7) For those who build new ships and demolish old ships, rewards will also be given for demolishing old ships to promote the improvement of ships and prevent them from being purchased by foreigners. (8) The amount of the reward for building a new ship is approximately 6-7% of the cost. If an old ship is demolished at the same time, the bonus received can account for 12% of the cost of the new ship. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Legislative Yuan Plans to Build New Site

(Nanjing) President Sun [Fo] stated that the construction of a new site for the Legislative Yuan in the central political district has been approved by the National Government, which has allocated more than 400,000 yuan for construction expenses. A New Site Construction Committee has now been formed, consisting of Liang Han Cao, Wu Jingxiong, Fu Bingchang, Ma Yinchu, Wu Shangying, and He Sui, to be responsible for actively carrying out the project. Liang invited the members on the 18th to discuss and solicit plans for the new site. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Drafting Process of the Baojia Statute

(Nanjing) During the review of the Baojia Statute at the Legislative Yuan on the 18th, many members raised objections. As a result, the text of the draft was revised and passed. It consists of forty-two articles. Huang Youchang reported in detail on the drafting process of the case, stating briefly that Articles 1 to 9 stipulate the organization of Baojia and the census; Articles 10 to 20 stipulate the personnel of Baojia and their tasks; Articles 21 and 22 stipulate the matters that should be stipulated in the Baojia rules and, when necessary, the joint guarantee and joint liability pledge; Articles 23 to 29 stipulate the training, organization, and exemptions of the militia; Articles 30 to 32 stipulate the Baojia expenses; Articles 33 to 38 stipulate penalties and commendations; and Articles 39 to 42 stipulate the incidental matters arising from this statute. In summary, there are six key points: (1) The Baojia Statute is generated from Article 74 of the County Autonomy Law. Previously, Baojia and autonomy were completely integrated. Therefore, the organization below the township level in counties and below the district level in cities will be changed from neighborhoods to Baojia in order to achieve uniformity. However, the implementation of affairs arising from the organization of Baojia in cities and counties is inherently difficult to unify, and there seems to be no need to force uniformity. Therefore, following the example of Article 111 of the draft constitution, when cities need to organize Baojia, the provisions of this statute may be applied mutatis mutandis. (2) According to the County Autonomy Law, the township is a level below the county, and there has been no change due to the implementation of the Baojia system. It has no impact on the use of the four rights of the people in handling autonomous affairs and training the people. Before the completion of autonomy, according to the current facts, the Jia head is publicly elected by the heads of households in the Jia, and the Bao head is publicly elected by the Jia heads in the Bao. When autonomy has achieved considerable results and the people have been trained to use the four rights, the Baojia head will be elected by the citizens in the Baojia under the jurisdiction of the township head, which is still consistent with the principle of citizen-based autonomy. As for the organization method based on households, it is stipulated based on the fifth theory of nationalism and the patriarchal system in the family law of the Civil Code. It will not change due to the different stages of supporting autonomy, starting autonomy, and completing autonomy. (3) Conducting a census is one of the six methods for starting to implement local autonomy and is also the main task of the current Baojia system. Therefore, there are regulations for conducting a census first when organizing Baojia. (4) The revision of militia training to civil training, as well as the regulations on training subjects and teaching materials, are based on the principles of implementing civil training recently passed by the Central and Local Autonomy Planning Committee. (5) The joint guarantee and joint liability pledge are limited to being carried out only when necessary. The Bao head should strive to reduce the fines for residents in the Bao, and the security team should be abolished in stages. All of this is aimed at achieving autonomy and self-defense and adjusting in practice and implementing in theory, so as to be beneficial to practical use and facilitate the promotion of autonomy. Therefore, the nature of the Baojia Statute produced by the Autonomy Law is slightly different from that of the Baojia Statute for organizing and checking households produced in the bandit suppression area. (6) The implementation rules of this statute are formulated by the provincial governments with reference to local conditions, indicating that they are flexible and provide general regulations. The County Defense Corps Law has been abolished in accordance with the principles of the central and local autonomy laws and regulations. When the city needs to organize Baojia, the county regulations shall apply mutatis mutandis, and there is no need to draft another set of regulations. Previous accumulated cases such as the revised County and City Defense Corps Law should be revoked. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Hebei-Chahar General Inspection Office Temporarily Does Not Collect Inspection Fees; Li Qingxuan Issues Written Statement

(Tianjin) Wang Hong'en, Director of the Hebei-Chahar General Inspection Office, notified various agencies on the 18th, stating that he has taken office. The office will not charge fees for inspecting goods for the time being, only register them first. The Ronin Trade Association and smuggling shops will be responsible for allowing the goods to be transported and sold first, and the fees will be collected later after the fee rates are determined. On the 18th, Li Qingxuan again visited Xu Liya, Sun Weidong, Wang Hong'en, Guo Zhihan, and Qin Dechun to discuss the cooperation of Hebei-Chahar in suppressing smuggling and the collection of inspection fees by the Hebei-Chahar General Inspection Office. Opinions are gradually becoming consistent. In order to avoid hindering the collection of customs duties, the inspection fee for smuggled goods will be collected at the highest rate. Li will return south to report after the negotiations in Tianjin are completed. (Special dispatch, 18th)

(Jinan) Representative Song's representative Li Shijun returned from Jibei after passing through Jinan and said that Finance Minister Kong [Xiangxi] is very understanding about the Hebei-Chahar Inspection Office. (Special dispatch, 18th)

(Jinan) In recent days, a large number of smuggled goods have been transported from Tianjin to Jinan by car. (Special dispatch, 18th)

(Tianjin) In a written statement issued on the 18th, Qingxuan stated that he came north last month to meet Song and discussed the situation in the Tianjin market. He had previously instructed [me] to return to Minister Kong to present his opinions. After research by the competent department, he returned with [these opinions] to discuss [them]. He visited Song on the 17th and reported on the progress. On the original proposed method, [Song] still instructed [him] to study it in detail with the relevant personnel in order to seek a suitable way to maintain the interests of Chinese and foreign merchants and enable the economy of North China to become active day by day. It is not exclusively for the problem of the Hebei-Chahar Inspection Office. This office was reorganized from the Cangzhou Salt and Coast Defense Inspection Office and has been established for a long time to inspect bandits, drugs, and military supplies and to assist in suppressing smuggling. It was not established for the purpose of collecting consumption taxes. Now the truth has been clarified, and there is no need for further research. (Special dispatch, 18th)

Finance Minister Kong Discusses Recent Financial and Diplomatic Situation; Advantages of Income Tax Are Equal Burden; Financial and Monetary Conditions in Guangdong and Guangxi Can Gradually Get on the Right Track; Sino-Japanese Diplomatic Negotiations Based on Equality and Mutual Benefit

Vice President of the Executive Yuan Kong visited Zhang Qun at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at 4:00 p.m. on the 18th to discuss matters. He took a car to Shanghai at 5:00 p.m. Since President Jiang [Jieshi] personally took charge in Guangdong to handle the Guangdong-Guangxi incident, Kong has been acting on behalf of the President of the Executive Yuan for two months. Reporters, concerned about the recent progress in finance and diplomacy, which has attracted general attention, visited the Executive Yuan before Kong's departure to Shanghai, and he kindly issued the following statement. The reporter first asked about the income tax issue. Kong said, "Our country's tax system has always focused on indirect taxes, and the unequal burden has long been criticized by scholars. The decision to implement income tax and inheritance tax is truly a new era in the history of our country's tax system. The Inheritance Tax Law is currently being drafted, and the Income Tax Law will be implemented next month. There are many advantages to income tax. The most important is the equal burden. Indirect taxes do not distinguish between rich and poor, and everyone pays taxes equally. There is even the strange phenomenon that the poor pay more and the rich pay less. Income tax is not only consistent with morality, law, and human sentiment, but also a scientific and modern tax system, which is fully in line with the principle of controlling capital in Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. In addition, income tax is also related to the completion of the legal tender policy. Since the implementation of the legal tender policy last year, it has been effective. However, in order to maximize its benefits, fiscal revenue and expenditure must be balanced. The method of balancing revenue and expenditure is nothing more than increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. Implementing income tax is the best way to increase revenue. In recent times, European and American countries have all used income tax as a major source of national treasury revenue, which is clear evidence. Therefore, implementing income tax can improve the tax system, reduce the burden on the poor, enrich the national treasury, and increase the credit of legal tender. It has a significant relationship with finance and monetary affairs. The collection procedures will also adopt simple methods. Observing that the national patriotic concepts of the people have been increasing in recent years, there should be no need to worry about boring tax evasion behaviors in the future. As for foreign residents in China, they have long been accustomed to paying income tax and enjoy all kinds of rights in our country. Based on the principle of balancing rights and obligations, they should be able to assess the situation, weigh the pros and cons, and accept this legal and reasonable income tax." The reporter asked about the financial and monetary reorganization situation in Guangdong and Guangxi. Kong said that he has always attached great importance to the finances of Guangdong and Guangxi and had conducted investigations early on. Since the promulgation of the Provisional Measures for Reorganizing Finance in Guangdong, the currency system, exchange rates, and prices in Guangdong Province have tended to stabilize, and finance has gradually become active. Guangdong is a place where overseas Chinese capital is concentrated. From now on, remittances from overseas Chinese will come in steadily, and the development of industry and commerce can be expected soon. Guangxi has always been known as barren. Over the years, Li [Zongren], Bai [Chongxi], and others have painstakingly managed it, and finance has a considerable foundation. Now that it has been unified, the financial and monetary conditions can gradually get on the right track, and there should be no problem. The decision to properly solve the financial and monetary problems in Guangdong and Guangxi is half the fortune of the people of Guangdong and Guangxi, and the country's entire finance and monetary affairs will also benefit from it. The reporter then talked about central finance. Kong said that he has been in charge of finance for three years and has lived in hardship every day. Fortunately, with the guidance of the President and the cooperation and hard work of central and local officials and people, he has managed to cope. This year, God blesses China. After the unification of the national government orders, the harvest is abundant, and the disaster is spared. The future of finance and monetary affairs will be easier to deal with than before. We should still maintain the spirit of hard work in the past, not be arrogant or indulgent, and continue to work hard. Later, the reporter talked about the establishment of an inspection office in Hebei-Chahar. The reporter said that since the customs has been earnestly suppressing smuggling, smuggling merchants have gradually disappeared. The sudden rumor that Hebei-Chahar will set up an office to collect taxes will inevitably revive the smuggling trend. What is the purpose of this, and what should be done to cope with it? Kong said that Tianjin is an area where goods converge. There are indeed a considerable number of unscrupulous merchants colluding with Ronin to smuggle goods. There are also many ignorant merchants who temporarily seek private gain, do not understand the interests of the country, and purchase and hoard smuggled goods. The Hebei-Chahar authorities' efforts to provide relief are indeed intended to sympathize with ignorant merchants, and their intention is commendable. The Ministry of Finance has now sent personnel to Ping [Beiping] to discuss everything. As long as the prestige of the government's laws and regulations can be preserved, and the customs administration, commercial treaties, and the interests of legitimate chambers of commerce across the country are not affected, temporary relief measures can be properly drafted. The central government will not disagree. The Hebei-Chahar authorities are no less patriotic than others and will not lightly believe in a few small and biased petitions, resulting in the loss of their original intention. Finally, the reporter asked about the progress of Sino-Japanese diplomatic negotiations. Kong said that China and Japan are brotherly countries and should have been on good terms with each other and jointly maintain peace in East Asia. Unfortunately, various disputes in the past have deviated from this purpose. For several years, both sides have been in trouble. Recently, the authorities of both countries have clearly expressed their willingness to seek adjustments in Sino-Japanese relations so that the diplomacy between the two countries can be put on the right track. Unexpectedly, just as the negotiations were about to begin, the Chengdu and Beihai tragedies occurred one after another, injuring innocent people. We deeply regret this. Ambassador Kawagoe [Shigeru] to China came to Beijing to discuss this incident and general Sino-Japanese diplomatic issues. The competent authorities should follow the central government's intention, be friendly, open, and frank, and negotiate candidly. It is hoped that the Japanese side can also uphold the position of maintaining peace in East Asia and jointly seek adjustments to all issues between China and Japan on the principle of equality and mutual benefit. The future of both countries depends deeply on this. (Central News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Yu Hanmou Holds Banquet for Hong Kong Governor; Grand Banquet Held at British Consulate; Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Attends in Person

The Beihai Zhongye Case: Initial Investigation Proves Difficult; Ling Shifen's Brief Visit to Beihai Yields No Results; Returns to the Provincial Capital to Report and is Ordered to Return by Ship

Guangzhou Dispatch: Regarding the Beihai Zhongye case, the Japanese side has recently been eager to investigate the matter, repeatedly inquiring about methods. However, Diao Zuqian, the special envoy for foreign affairs of Guangdong and Guangxi, stated that government authority does not extend to Beihai. The Lianzhou area is still garrisoned by Weng Zhaoyuan's Guangxi army, which has not yet withdrawn. Therefore, the first step in the investigation of the case has not been completed, and negotiations cannot begin. According to recent observations, a detailed investigation can only begin after the Beihai garrison under Weng Zhaoyuan withdraws. Previously, Ling Shifen, secretary of the special envoy's office for foreign affairs, along with Yang Bingli, secretary of the provincial government, and two others, arrived in Beihai aboard the Fu'an warship. Although they briefly landed, they were constrained by circumstances and could not investigate. They hastily returned to the ship and reported to the provincial capital, requesting instructions. According to news from Lianzhou, when Ling and Yang arrived in Beihai on the morning of the 12th, landing was extremely difficult. The Beihai defense forces feared that Ling and Yang would collude with the Japanese in Beihai, leading to a second disturbance. Therefore, after local military officers received a telegram from the provincial government dispatching Ling and Yang to investigate, they deployed troops along the Beihai embankment, strictly inspecting incoming travelers and refusing to allow suspected individuals to disembark. When the Fu'an ship docked, Ling and Yang first submitted a list of names to the local military officers, declaring that no Japanese were accompanying them, before being allowed to land. That morning, Ling and Yang transferred from the Fu'an warship to a Beihai Customs electric boat and landed via the Customs wharf. The wharf was surrounded by sentries, and machine guns were set up nearby, as if facing a major enemy. After landing, they were still unable to move freely. Later, they requested Qiu Guozhen, chief of staff of Weng's division, and Zhong Junsheng, director of the Beihai Municipal Bureau, to guide them. Ling and Yang were then able to rest briefly at the Municipal Bureau. The public followed Ling and Yang to the Municipal Bureau and sent representatives to meet with them, inquiring about the purpose of their visit. Ling and Yang, understanding their intentions, could only reply that they had been ordered to investigate the Zhongye case. At the same time, they reported that a Japanese warship had arrived, and the government, to prevent further incidents, had rushed to dissuade the Japanese warship's investigators from landing lightly and to wait for our investigation. After Ling and Yang announced this, seeing the tense atmosphere in the city, they knew that the investigation would not be easy to initiate. They were forced to return to the Fu'an warship and first notified the Japanese warship Sagayama by signal flag, advising them to stay outside the port temporarily. They then telegraphed the provincial government to request instructions from Diao, the special envoy for foreign affairs. They soon received a reply, ordering them to return to the provincial capital first. Ling and Yang then returned to the provincial capital aboard the original ship on the morning of the 14th to report. The Fu'an warship arrived in Hong Kong on the morning of the 15th, where it purchased coal. To hasten their report, Ling and Yang no longer traveled by ship but instead took the Guangzhou-Kowloon express train to the province that morning, arriving in Guangzhou at 11:00 a.m. They immediately went to see Diao Zuqian, reported on their experience in Beihai, and stated that the Beihai garrison was not responsible for protecting the investigation, which was the greatest difficulty in the case. Therefore, the primary issue was to first order the withdrawal of the Beihai defense forces, and then the case could be investigated. Diao considered this to be within the scope of military administration and, on the morning of the 16th, at 9:00 a.m., accompanied Ling and Yang to visit Huang Musong, chairman of the provincial government, and Yu Hanmou, commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, requesting them to quickly negotiate with the Beihai defense forces for a withdrawal as soon as possible or to assume responsibility for protection to facilitate diplomatic progress. This was accepted. Diao, believing that there was news of the withdrawal of the Beihai garrison, then dispatched Ling Shifen again on the morning of the 17th aboard the Fu'an warship to Beihai for a second time to continue the investigation, seeking the truth on which to base diplomatic negotiations. Meanwhile, Japanese Consul-General ad interim to Guangdong, Yoshitake Sadaharu, upon hearing that our investigator Ling Shifen had returned to the provincial capital, personally visited the office of the special envoy for foreign affairs of Guangdong and Guangxi that morning (the 16th) to inquire about news. Diao reported in detail on the situation of the first investigators in Beihai. The Japanese consul also expressed his views, and the two sides discussed for a long time before the Japanese consul departed. (September 17th)

Northeastern People in the Past Five Years Endure Oppression from the Enemy, Their Lives Plunging into Despair

Shenyang Dispatch: After seizing the Northeast, the Japanese immediately began to massively relocate farmers from Japan to villages in the Northeast. Using political power, they forcibly confiscated land from native farmers and cultivated it themselves, causing the native farmers to lose their livelihoods and fall into despair, with their food and clothing exhausted. This is the first aspect. The sale and purchase of agricultural products in the Northeast are monopolized by Japanese-established companies, which frequently lower prices according to their needs, causing serious damage to the remaining farmers and leading many to bankruptcy. This is the second aspect. In preparation for war against the Soviet Union, the Japanese have spared no effort in constructing military railways over the past five years. Wherever they pass, they unconditionally confiscate land and houses from native farmers, leaving them with nowhere to live. This is the third aspect. This is a general overview of the Japanese oppression of farmers in the Northeast. As for the oppression of workers, after the September 18th Incident, national industries in the Northeast suffered from the attack of Japanese merchants and withered like autumn leaves. Laborers and workers who previously relied on these industries for their livelihoods are now wandering the streets, becoming starving corpses. Some who work in factories opened by the Japanese receive treatment far different from that of Japanese workers. For example, Japanese skilled workers in yarn factories and coal mines can earn an average of about 30 yuan per month, working eight hours a day. In contrast, Chinese workers toil hard for ten or twelve hours or more each day, earning at most only 3 jiao or so per day. It goes without saying that their meager income is insufficient to support their families. However, that is not all. In addition to this cruel economic exploitation, they also suffer from a kind of extra-economic political oppression. For example, workers in factories are not allowed to talk to more than two companions at a time, otherwise they are considered troublemakers and dismissed. Workers are not allowed to organize or join labor unions and are not allowed to move freely. They must permanently reside in workshops near the factory, paying a fixed rent each month. If workers gather in groups of five or three, they are considered to be holding meetings and are followed and monitored by Japanese police, even arrested. As for female and child laborers, their exploitation is even more tragic. Child laborers usually work about 14 hours a day, receiving only 2 jiao or no pay at all. The same is true for female laborers, who must also endure the trampling and humiliation of Japanese foremen, daring not to speak out. Their tragic fate is often too unbearable to describe. This is a general outline of the oppression suffered by the majority of workers. As for capitalists and entrepreneurs, due to the flooding of the market with Japanese goods and the cessation of sales of domestic goods, the factories and companies they operate have been forcibly bought by the Japanese side, making it impossible to operate, and they have all fallen into bankruptcy. As for young students, they are denied freedom of thought and freedom of education, and they are readily labeled as communists and killed without exception. Their cruelty is even more unnecessary to describe in detail.

Hebei and Chahar: Candidates for the Economic Council are Being Sought; Li Sihao and Zhang Hu Have No Intention of Accepting the Position; Wang Kemin's Resignation Has Not Yet Been Approved

Tianjin Dispatch: Regarding the North China economic development matter, after Wang Kemin's visit to the North was thwarted and he angrily resigned, the Japanese military's stance on this matter has shifted from direct to indirect, only urging the Hebei and Chahar authorities to find a suitable person to take charge of the Economic Council. At the same time, they also hope that the person responsible has a considerable connection with the current regime in North China, which would be more appropriate. Regarding Wang Kemin personally, apart from the faction of staff officers Wachi and Senta, who are strongly opposed, Commander Tadai, Chief of Staff Hashimoto, Director of the Ikeda Economic Advisory Department, and others mostly hold a more moderate view. Last week, the Tokyo military sent a telegram to Tianjin regarding this matter, giving instructions to the garrison headquarters. Tadai and Hashimoto specially summoned Wachi and Senta to inform them, so the anti-Wang atmosphere has subsided recently. Even the colored newspapers under the direction of certain individuals are not attacking and slandering him with the same force as before. Song Zheyuan personally has no preconceived notions about Wang, but too many of his aides are acting out of self-interest, fearing that Wang's rise to power would be detrimental to them and that Wang would seize economic power, thus restricting their actions. Therefore, they have been the most vocal in inciting opposition. However, after Wang's resignation, the situation in North China is as it is, and Song is surrounded by his aides. No one with foresight dares to come. Therefore, although Song has received Wang's resignation letter, he has not yet expressed his opinion. During a banquet for Wang at the Bei Ning official residence on Haihe Road on the evening of the 15th, he spoke of other matters, neither approving the resignation nor expressing his desire to retain him. It is widely rumored that Song is looking for a successor and will only announce his approval of Wang's resignation when a replacement is found. At this juncture, it is rumored that there are three internally decided candidates: Li Sihao, Zhang Hu, and Zhang Shizhao. Li Sihao was invited to the North this spring, and he met with Song once, but the result was unfavorable, and he quietly returned to the South. Li refused to take the position, so Wang Kemin was considered. Now Li is being considered again. According to those close to him here, he has no intention of going north, regretting that Wang Kemin was manipulated by others. Zhang Hu has abandoned his political career in recent years and is not engaged in any activities. His mind is like still water, and he is even less willing to change his simple life for a temporary impulse. As for Zhang Shizhao, he came to Tianjin to appear in court for the case of acting as an agent for a Russian woman's inheritance, and he has not yet left. Although he is not an economic expert, some believe that he has the talent to be a long-sleeved dancer and have recommended him to Song. On the afternoon of the 16th, at 3:00 p.m., Song, accompanied by Chen Juesheng, director of the Bei Ning Railway Bureau, personally visited his residence on Penglai Street in the Japanese concession to discuss and exchange views. That evening, at 7:00 p.m., he hosted a banquet at the Bei Ning official residence on Haihe Road, inviting Zhang Zizhong and Chen Zhongfu as guests. Judging from the situation, if neither Li nor Zhang can be moved and Wang's resignation cannot be reversed, then as a last resort, this person may be used as a replacement. As for whether he can open up diplomatic avenues depends on Zhang's personal skills.

Regarding the economic development plan, we would very much like the Japanese side to draw up a plan so that there are restrictions, to avoid endless demands in the future and being exhausted in dealing with them. However, the Japanese side is in favor of gradual progress, without being subject to any restrictions. Any discovery will be regarded as a source of economic development. For example, the newly established General Audit Office of the Hebei-Chahar Council is levying new taxes, which is also a current issue in economic cooperation. However, the Japanese side is reluctant to record it and list it in the requested items. In fact, they are more eager for it than any other event. Therefore, it is not easy for Song to find a person to take on this role, which is in between diplomacy, economics, and politics. On the afternoon of the 17th, at 3:00 p.m., Wang Kemin met with Song Zheyuan at No. 133, 17th Road, in the British concession. They talked for an hour. Song only expressed to Wang, "In the current situation, everything is difficult to handle. In the future, I still ask you to go to Peiping to assist in everything. It's good to be working for the country. Whether in power or in opposition, we must all work together." He still made no clear statement regarding Wang's resignation. (September 17th)

On this day, all entertainment venues in Suzhou were closed for one day, and all sectors flew flags at half-mast to express their condolences to the compatriots who died in the Northeast.

Changshu

Tragic Boat Capsizing in the Yangtze River

On the Yangtze River near the Dragon King Temple in Beixin Lock, Sixth District of the county, a seagoing vessel passed by the day before yesterday, fully loaded with bran cakes. It was sailing downstream from Zhenjiang to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, at around 3:00 p.m., a strong wind suddenly arose, and in an instant, a terrifying wave surged. The seagoing vessel became like a small leaf boat, with no one to steer it and no help to call for. As the wind was very strong, the ship lost its steering and capsized. All 22 people on board fell into the water at the same time and were swept away by the current. At that time, there was a lifeboat on the river. Seeing this scene, it hurriedly rowed to rescue them, but the white waves were overwhelming, the river surface was vast, and the wind and water were swift. Only one person was rescued. Afterwards, the leader of the Hushu security detachment sent a small boat to investigate and learned about the ship's losses, which were quite unfortunate.

Cook Dismissed from Post Commits Suicide

A young traveler suddenly committed suicide by poisoning himself at the Economic Hotel outside the South Gate on the 17th. After investigation, the traveler was identified as Zhang Bing, 30 years old, from out of town. He was originally a cook in the Second Precinct of the Public Security Bureau. Recently, due to a change of directors, a large number of patrol officers, inspectors, and directors of the branch bureau were changed, and Zhang Bing also lost his job. He lodged in the Economic Hotel, but soon ran out of money. As a result, he bought and ingested raw opium and committed suicide. The county government sent officials to examine the body and ordered the local bailiffs to bury it.

Robbery and Assault in Mengcheng Town

Zhu Renhong of Mengcheng Town, Third District of the county, runs a sundries store outside the Small South Gate, with a thriving business. Recently, he was coveted by criminals. Suddenly, on the night of the 15th, four bandits used stones to break open the main gate, each holding guns, knives, and wooden sticks, and entered the room to search and rob at will. The owner, Zhu Renhong, was beaten and injured. All gold, silver jewelry, sugar, and other items were looted. After half an hour, they left with a whoop. The district chief, Zhu Tianying, also sent personnel to investigate. On the 17th, they reported to the county government for joint arrest. County Chief Hou has sent detectives to the countryside to investigate the stolen goods and bring the criminals to justice.

Theft of Famous Paintings

Ding Keshu of Huaqing Lane in Zhongshan Gate of the county, the current leader of the Water Public Security Bureau detachment, is stationed outside, and his family has more than a hundred scrolls of ancient and famous paintings, worth more than 3,000 yuan. Only his wife, Zhang, is left to guard them. Recently, Zhang returned to Ning, and Tan Tiegong, who was living with her, sneaked in and stole all the paintings for sale, intending to flee to Beijing on the 17th. Zhang happened to return home on that day, discovered the previous situation, and immediately went to investigate. She found them at the Nanyang Hotel and searched out eight scrolls of calligraphy and painting. She reported to the Public Security Fifth Precinct for assistance. Tan Tiegong took advantage of the lack of preparation and escaped over the wall in the station. He was caught at the Zhencheng Highway Station after searching everywhere and is currently being interrogated.

Male and Female Teachers Sue for Divorce

Tao Kaoxu, the son of Tao Jingli of Jiwang Temple, Second District, and his daughter-in-law, Li Keying, are both elementary school teachers. They married four years ago, and their relationship has been poor. Now, Li is suing the county government for divorce, claiming that her husband is impotent and cannot satisfy her sexual desire. On the afternoon of the 16th, the single trial judge opened the trial and first advised the plaintiff that impotence can be treated and there is no need for divorce. Li testified that she had been treated without success and had been waiting for four and a half years and could not wait any longer, and demanded compensation for losses and alimony of 3,000 yuan. Tao testified that Li refused to have sex and was not impotent. Li testified that it was indeed a youth injury and could be examined. The court ordered Tao to prepare funds and send a document from the county to the Zhenru Forensic Institute for examination before further review.

National Society of the Principles of Life

Nanjing Dispatch: The National Society of the Principles of Life has been established in the capital for more than a year. Its purpose is to persuade people to abstain from tobacco and alcohol, eradicate all narcotic drugs and various bad habits, and secretly embrace the principles of the New Life Movement. In particular, it leads comrades of the Society of the Principles of Life in various provinces and cities to jointly organize a sound organization, which is taken very seriously. During the current registration period, there are some differences of opinion in various aspects. It is heard that the association deals with disputes of various subordinate associations impartially and resolves them through peaceful means, never adding coercive behavior. Whenever there is an unreasonable subordinate association with barbaric character, the association immediately submits the entire case to the Central Ministry of Public Training and applies for verification. Recently, Shao Zhiguang and Zhao Changchun of the Dongtai Society of the Principles of Life Branch Preparatory Office have been capricious and have attempted to coerce the association. The association has not compared itself with them and has ordered the subordinate association to return the registration certificates one by one and submit all the text of the subordinate association that insults the general association to the Central Government without concealment, showing that the association is frank and open. After the association presented to the Central Government, the Public Training Department of the Central Executive Committee instructed that the association's record be filed and approved the revocation of the Dongtai Society of the Principles of Life Branch.

Ningbo

Fire on Baizhang Road in Jiangdong

Fu Yihe Copper and Tin Shop, located at the intersection of Zhufang Street on Baizhang Road in Jiangdong, this port, is a property established by Chuan Dingyang himself. It has three buildings, front and rear, and has been operating for many years, and the business is doing well. In addition to two buildings for his own use, the remaining building is rented to Zhu Yongxing, a native of Shaoxing, as a warehouse, with fire insurance of 2,000 yuan. At about 3 pm yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out on the second floor of Fu Yihe, which quickly spread through the roof. All the dragons heard the alarm and rescued each other, and it was extinguished after more than an hour. It is estimated that two three-story buildings of Fu Yihe, one three-story building of Yongle Grocery Store, one three-story building of Bao Shunxing Qingji Xiang Store, one three-story building of Yu Songtao's Fate Hall, one three-story building of Minghua Watch Store, one three-story building of Bao Shunxing Shengxun Xiang Store, one three-story building of Shi Jintai, two three-story buildings of Yifa Laundry, one three-story building of Yipinxiang Noodle Shop, and one three-story building of Zhu Yongxing's warehouse on Zhongjie Street, one three-story building of Li Fufang, one empty building, and two demolished buildings were burned down. A total of fourteen three-story buildings were burned down and two were demolished, with a loss of no less than 20,000 yuan. Because most of the properties were self-owned, the cause of the fire was said to be caused by the residual fire of a cigarette butt. When the fire broke out, the female owner of Bao Shunxing fell from the building. Because she was pregnant, she was seriously injured and had been sent to the hospital for treatment.

Haizhou

Female Passenger Commits Suicide on Train

At about 5:00 p.m. yesterday (the 15th), on the Longhai slow train from Haizhou to Xinpu, a female passenger, about 20 years old, suddenly swallowed matches. A military police officer on the train saw this and immediately stopped her. When the train arrived at Xinpu Station, he asked her to get off the train and asked her name and why she committed suicide. The woman refused to tell the truth, only answering that her name was Li Xuezhi, she was 23 years old, and she was from Wanzai County, Jiangxi Province. A few days ago, she took a train from home to the Haizhou City Teachers College to look for a classmate but did not find him. The money on her side was exhausted, so she had the idea of ​​despairing of the world. The night before, she had attempted to hang herself unsuccessfully in a hotel in Haizhou City. This afternoon at 4:00 p.m., a police officer from the Public Security Bureau escorted me onto the train. At the same time, a tax police officer helped me with ten silver dollars to go to Lianyungang to find friends, so I committed suicide on the train again. The military police officer saw that she had swallowed a small number of matches and immediately persuaded her and told her not to commit suicide again. At about 7:00 p.m., the woman took the Longhai eastbound express train to Lianyungang.

Xiaoshan

Three Families Robbed in One Night in Four Villages

Recently, in the Shadi area of Xiaoshan, due to the cotton market season, many households in the villages have accumulated money. As a result, bandits have been robbing households frequently. On the night of the 15th, around midnight, more than ten bandits speaking local dialect broke into the home of farmer Shen Kaiming near Nanyang and looted them extensively, resulting in a loss of 120 yuan. On the same night, a gang of seven bandits broke into the nearby home of Gao Hesheng, searched extensively, and stole 80 yuan in silver from the sale of cotton, plus clothing and accessories worth over 70 yuan. On the same night, at Ganlu Temple, the home of farmer Shi Kequan was robbed by more than ten bandits, who stole 37 yuan in banknotes from the sale of cotton, plus bedding and other items worth over 100 yuan. The area of Zhou Dong Village is remote and isolated, beyond the reach of military police. Families with slight savings are coveted by bandits, and there is a fear of not being able to sleep peacefully at night.

Bengbu

Joint Transportation by Huainan Railway and Shipping Industry

Since the opening of the Huainan Railway this year, it has not only facilitated coal transportation for the Huainan Mining Bureau, but also benefited cargo transportation and business travel in central Anhui. In order to develop its business and facilitate transportation, the Mining Bureau has recently partnered with the Bengbu Huaihe Shipping Cooperative to jointly operate passenger and freight transportation, with Tianji'an as the central hub for development. After thorough consultations with Chen Ruchen, the person in charge of the cooperative, a passenger and freight joint transportation contract was signed, and Chen was also hired as a coordinator for the Mining Bureau. The cooperative has five fast steamboats, which will begin operations on the 16th, with daily steamboat services between Bengbu and Tianji'an. Services will also be offered simultaneously at all stations along the Huainan Railway and at various wharves along the Huaihe River, with Tianji'an as the terminal for connecting transportation. Currently, the shipping cooperative is temporarily operating the Bengbu-Tianji'an route and will soon expand to the Tian-Zheng and Beng-Zheng (i.e., Zhengyangguan) routes. Preparations are already underway, and the plan has been submitted to the party and government organs for record-keeping. With the cooperation of boats and trains, it is expected that business development will be immeasurable.

News from Our Newspaper

Newly Appointed Ambassador to the Soviet Union Jiang Tingfu Paid a Visit to Soviet Ambassador Yesterday, Ambassador Bo Hosting a Banquet Tonight for Formal Reception

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, the newly appointed Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Dr. Jiang Tingfu, returned to Beijing after meeting with the former Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Dr. Yan Huiqing, in Qingdao. He attended a banquet hosted by Finance Minister Kong on the night before last and left Beijing on the 11:00 PM express train that night, arriving in Shanghai at around 7:00 AM yesterday. After disembarking, he went to the residence of his close relatives, the Xu family, in Pudong to rest.

Visit to Ambassador Bo

Around 10:00 AM, he drove to the Soviet Consulate General on Huangpu Road to visit the Soviet Ambassador to China, Mr. Bogomolov. The discussion lasted for half an hour before he departed. Ambassador Bo specifically scheduled a banquet at his residence at 8:30 PM tonight to entertain Mr. Jiang, and invited Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Zhou Jue, and others to accompany. This is the first formal reception between the two ambassadors since Mr. Jiang was appointed as the ambassador to the Soviet Union.

Welcoming Banquet Last Night

The Shanghai International Affairs Research Association held a special banquet at the Bank Club on Hong Kong Road at 7:30 PM last night to welcome Mr. Jiang. It was hosted by Chairman Guo Bingwen, with board members Li Zhaohuan, Liu Zhanen, Xu Xinliu, Jin Guobao, He Dekui, Kuang Yaokun, and over twenty others in attendance. First, Mr. Guo Bingwen delivered a welcoming speech on behalf of the association, and then Mr. Jiang gave a speech, briefly outlining his aspirations for his mission to the Soviet Union. The gathering ended at around 9:00 PM in high spirits. The Saturday Association is also scheduled to host a luncheon and speech for Mr. Jiang at the International Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road this afternoon, which Mayor Wu and others will attend.

Mr. Jiang's Remarks

A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency interviewed Mr. Jiang last night. According to him, the main purpose of his trip was to visit Soviet Ambassador Bo, which was only a courtesy visit. He is scheduled to return to Beijing on Sunday (i.e., tomorrow) and then return to his hometown of Baoqing, Hunan. He is scheduled to take a ship from Shanghai to Vladivostok at the end of next month to take office, but the exact date has not been determined, as he needs to consult with President Jiang for instructions before making a decision. As for the new embassy staff, as reported in the newspapers, one or two people will travel ahead of him. When asked about his aspirations for his mission to the Soviet Union, Mr. Jiang said that the task of any foreign representative is to investigate and study the situation in the host country and report to their own government. If his investigation report is incorrect, he is responsible. The government will decide on the policy. Matters related to Sino-Soviet trade have always been conducted by Soviet Ambassador Bo in our country, and Ambassador Bo will continue to conduct them with our authorities in the future.

Contemporary Figures

Kong Xiangxi left Beijing yesterday afternoon on a special express train with a sleeper car attached, arriving in Shanghai at 10:50 PM last night. He disembarked at the Zhenru station.

Sun Ke left Beijing on a special express train last night, arriving in Shanghai at 7:00 AM this morning.

Soviet Ambassador to China, Mr. Bogomolov, hosted a banquet at the Soviet Consulate General at 1 Huangpu Road yesterday at noon to entertain representatives from all walks of life in our country. International Affairs Research Association Held a Tea Party Yesterday

Welcoming Zhu Xuefan and Shou Yicheng, Bidding Farewell to Yang Yinpu and Xu Gongsu

The International Affairs Research Association held a tea party yesterday at 5:00 PM at the Bank Club on Hong Kong Road to welcome Zhu Xuefan, our country's labor representative who recently attended the International Labor Conference, and Shou Yicheng, who returned from studying in Japan. They also bid farewell to Yang Yinpu and Xu Gongsu, commissioners dispatched by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the League of Nations Office. Apart from Zhu Xuefan, who was unable to attend due to business, Shou Yicheng, Yang Yinpu, Xu Gongsu, Guo Bingwen, Zhu Shaoping, Li Zhaohuan, Xu Peihuan, Wu Kaisheng, Liu Yunfang, Lin Kanghou, Wu Songgao, Huang Renzhi, Zhao Shutong, Cheng Haifeng, Cao Yunxiang, Li Yunliang, Shen Xinqing, Wu Guanghan, Jin Guobao, and others attended. After Chairman Guo Bingwen delivered a speech, Yang Yinpu, Xu Gongsu, Shou Yicheng, and Wu Songgao, Director of the International Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, gave speeches. The event ended at around 7:00 PM. The contents of their speeches are recorded below.

Mr. Yang's Speech

Yang Yinpu's speech briefly stated that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs appointed an economic commissioner to the League of Nations Office in Geneva because it is a central point for international affairs. His tasks are: (1) to prepare and collect various materials, such as those related to law and economics, etc.; (2) to collect foreign materials to meet domestic needs; (3) to introduce domestic materials to meet foreign needs; (4) to conduct on-the-spot investigations of the economies of various countries. The above four points are his direct tasks. His indirect tasks include research on the overall relationship of the international economy. The international situation is very complex, either dividing or uniting. For example, the Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan, dumping of coal and oil in Europe and the United States, and joining the League of Nations are trends of dividing and then uniting. Therefore, it is necessary to conduct thorough research on the world's economic situation.

Mr. Xu's Speech

Xu Gongsu's speech briefly stated that we should not have extremely high hopes for the League of Nations, but we should not underestimate it either. Because it is indeed an organization that maintains peace and promotes international cooperation. Before war or conflict breaks out between countries, the League of Nations can try to mediate. If war or conflict occurs, because the League of Nations' power is limited, it is impossible to expect the League of Nations to impose sanctions. The League of Nations should maintain world peace and promote various forms of cooperation through alliances. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs of our country attaches great importance to the League of Nations. This decision to dispatch an economic commissioner to the League of Nations Office is to jointly cooperate in researching the world economy.

Mr. Shou's Speech

Shou Yicheng's speech briefly stated that this time, he led a team to Japan to investigate the banking system in preparation for reorganizing the Central Bank. At the same time, he also took the opportunity to investigate the general situation. The economic issues between China and Japan are very complex. It is necessary to study how to adjust Sino-Japanese relations, especially economic diplomacy with Japan. Since the coup in Japan, its national policy has also been undergoing transformation. Japanese businessmen's observations of the puppet Manchuria are that those who are familiar with the world's economic situation also consider the situation to be complex, so those who invest in the puppet Manchuria are also particularly cautious.

Mr. Wu's Speech

Wu Songgao's speech briefly stated: (1) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has established a League of Nations Special Committee to connect the League of Nations and China. It will first establish an economic commissioner, and then establish a legal commissioner, etc. It is hoped that each commissioner will fully develop their tasks and establish close relations with the League of Nations, seeking cooperation technically. (2) Since the September 18th Incident, people generally believe that the League of Nations is too weak. However, it should be clear that the League of Nations cannot prevent wars and conflicts. The League of Nations is a maintainer of peace. The methods of studying the League of Nations issues are: (1) to improve general international knowledge; (2) to find ways to publicize the international situation, such as publishing publications, so that people can understand; (3) to connect international emotions and assist the government's diplomacy.

Indigenous Cloth Movement: 5th Anniversary Commemorative Meeting Yesterday, Approximately 500 Representatives from Various Agencies Attended, with Indigenous Cloth on Display for All Sectors to Observe

Yesterday marked the 5th anniversary of the Indigenous Cloth Movement. The China Native Products Promotion Association held a special 5th anniversary commemorative meeting at the Chongnong Hall in Huangwu, Zhuanqiao, on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway. Approximately 500 people attended, including association members, representatives from various agencies and organizations, farmers, and farm women. Ru Bocai, Jiang Bi, Zhao Hualong, Wang Guanchang, and others served as hosts. In addition to various indigenous cloths, photos, and inscriptions were displayed in the auditorium for all sectors to observe. At 6:30 AM, the meeting was called to order with the ringing of a bell. Zhang Yi presided over the meeting, Qian Zhengfang served as the recorder, and Zhang Nanshan served as the master of ceremonies. After the formalities were completed, the chairman delivered a report, stating in brief that the indigenous cloth movement is a movement to save the country and a movement to revive the nation. Central Committee member Wu Zhihui once said that the indigenous cloth movement is indeed a movement related to the survival of China. The Premier believed that this was an important task to solve the people's livelihood problem, and he spoke earnestly about it in his lectures on the Three Principles of the People. This movement began in September of the 20th year of the Republic of China and has lasted for five years. Thanks to the advocacy of the political authorities and the support of people from all walks of life, it has achieved considerable success. Not only are those who wear indigenous cloth not ashamed, but also the production of indigenous cloth has greatly improved. The government's protection of the development of the indigenous cloth industry has been meticulous. Indigenous cloth movement exhibitions and other activities in various provinces and regions are often reported in the newspapers, which have contributed to the spirit, economy, and national defense. At this time when the countryside is declining and the lives of farmers are in deep water, and foreign forces are becoming increasingly powerful, we should strive to promote the popularity of indigenous cloth, based on the determination to promote indigenous cloth, and move forward for the entire national salvation work, so that we will not fail the grand commemoration of today. Representatives from various sectors, including Cai Zaoshi and Ru Xiaojiang, gave speeches, which were very exciting. At 8:40 AM, the meeting was adjourned with slogans. The slogans are recorded below: (1) Promote indigenous cloth to save the countryside, (2) Promote indigenous cloth to revive the nation, (3) Promote indigenous cloth to advocate frugality, (4) Promote indigenous cloth to stop waste, (5) Compatriots, let's all rise up to promote indigenous cloth, (6) Compatriots, let's all rise up to wear indigenous cloth, (7) Long live the indigenous cloth movement, (8) Long live the Chinese nation. The association also prepared more than 5,000 slogans promoting indigenous cloth and posted them in various villages to encourage the public. The Shanghai County Indigenous Cloth Wearing Association should also take this opportunity to solicit members. The future of indigenous cloth has infinite hope.

Hebei-Chahar Political Council's Reply to the Chamber of Commerce Explains the Nature of the Inspection Office

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously inquired about the truth of the matter after the Hebei-Chahar Political Council established the Hebei-Chahar Inspection Office, fearing that it would help the circulation of smuggled goods. The reply from the Political Council is as follows: To the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, your telegram has been received. The trend of smuggling has recently become more rampant. North China is in an extraordinary position, and it is even more inappropriate to adopt a laissez-faire policy. If smuggled goods are not cleared by law, the customs may not be able to reach them. Therefore, in order to comply with the business community's wishes and adapt to local conditions, it is proposed to change the inspection offices in the Cang Salt and Coastal Defense ports into the Hebei-Chahar Inspection Office to inspect various smuggled goods. The scope of inspection is limited to smuggled goods that have already landed and leaked out, in other words, those that have crossed the customs line and are being transported or have entered the hands of inland merchants. It should not affect customs revenue. This measure has not yet been implemented and is originally intended to assist in anti-smuggling. Once the inspection is in place, existing goods will not be detained and affect commerce, and future goods will be alerted and gradually reduced. It will be stopped in three or four months and is not a permanent measure. As for the establishment of the Cang Salt and Coastal Defense port inspection offices, they were only for investigating and cracking down on smuggling and did not collect taxes. The newspaper report that taxes were collected at one-eighth of the customs duty is purely a rumor and does not conform to the facts. Please do not believe it. Answering your inquiry, the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, seal of the council.

The Social Affairs Bureau Announced the Provisional Measures for Boiler Inspection Yesterday. Factories Equipped with Boilers Must Register and Obtain Qualification Certificates from the Inspection Section

The Shanghai Provisional Measures for Boiler Inspection, after being approved by the municipal government, were officially announced by the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday in Notice No. 1624: "1. Industrial disasters are most easily caused by boiler explosions. Therefore, various European and American countries have formulated inspection regulations for the use of boilers and take precautions. In accordance with Article 27 of the Factory Safety and Hygiene Inspection Rules promulgated by the Ministry of Industry, the Provisional Measures for Boiler Inspection in this city are hereby formulated and submitted to the municipal government for approval in Instruction No. 20288. They will be implemented from today. This order is hereby announced for public information. Director-General Pan Gongzhan, September 18, 25th year of the Republic of China." The measures were reported in the September 12th newspaper and are omitted here. The Inspection Section of the Third Division of the Bureau has been ordered to comply. Factories equipped with boilers must apply for registration and obtain a qualification certificate from the Bureau before they can be used. The certificate specifies the name of the mechanical technician, the location of the office, the inspection date, and the validity period.

Zhejiang Local Bank Trial Operation of Farmer and Fisherman Loans, Effective in Yuqian, Yin County, Yuhuan and Other Counties, Now Decided to Find Ways to Promote and Make it Universal Throughout the Province

In addition to handling various agricultural loans, the Zhejiang Local Bank also tried to operate farmer and fisherman loans, which have been quite effective. It has now been decided to find ways to promote and make it universal throughout the province. The report is recorded below.

Farmer Loans

The bank, in view of the remote location, poor land, and poverty of the people in Qian County, and the long-standing economic distress of the countryside, signed a loan agreement with the county's Farmers Lending Office in the autumn of the 23rd year to cooperate in handling farmer loans in the county. With the enthusiastic advocacy of the county's party and government authorities, it has progressed smoothly over the past three years. According to statistics, more than 2,000 yuan was loaned out in the winter of the 23rd year, which was not much and the amount was small, all to meet the short-term emergency needs of farmers. In the spring of the 24th year, 30,000 yuan was loaned out for spring ploughing, with more than 700 mutual aid societies benefiting. Its effectiveness has spread to famous villages throughout the county. In the winter of that year, more than 6,000 yuan was loaned out under guarantee, and all were repaid on time and in full, with good results. In April of this year, the bank continued to handle seedling loans of more than 30,000 yuan, targeting more than 470 cooperative preparatory societies. In the future, the bank plans to focus on propaganda of cooperation and training of cooperative talents, so that cooperative preparatory societies can be reorganized into formal cooperative societies. It also plans to investigate the county's production industries to prepare for the organization of cooperative marketing. Furthermore, in view of the fact that Yin County has no financial institutions and farmers have a strong need for capital adjustment, the bank signed an agreement with the county government in the spring of the 24th year. Before the county's agricultural financial agency is formally established, the bank will provide funds and handle farmer loans throughout the county. The two parties will work together to carry out rural relief work and promulgate farmer loan rules based on the bank's agricultural and industrial loan regulations. The target of loans is mainly cooperative societies, but before cooperative society organizations are widely established, special farmer loans (i.e., individual farmer loans) may be handled. Borrowers are purely individual farmers, and all matters such as registration and investigation are handled by the county government, while the bank is responsible for lending. At that time, the bank had already loaned out a portion of cooperative loans in the county, so the portion handled on behalf of the county was almost entirely individual farmer loans, totaling more than 560 households, with each household borrowing a minimum of 10 yuan and a maximum of 50 yuan, for a total of about 20,000 yuan. All were repaid after the autumn harvest. It will continue to be handled this year and will be expanded slightly, with the amount increased to more than 110,000 yuan. Currently, Fenghua and other places have also signed agreements with the local county government to handle the matter according to the above method.

Fisherman Loans

Yuhuan is located by the sea, and most of its residents rely on fishing for a living. However, every time it is time to go to sea to fish, each fisherman needs considerable funds to repair his fishing boat and provide food for his family. The source of these funds has always been the local fishermen's association, which lends money to fishermen at a fixed interest rate. However, the interest rate is very high, and fishermen feel oppressed. Although the temporary difficulties are solved, the difficulties of the future are not alleviated. Not only that, but the oppression of fishermen is so deep that the development of the entire fishing industry is stagnant, which has a profound impact on the future of the fishing industry. The Yongjia Administrative Inspectorate, in view of this, consulted with the bank on lending as a way to remedy the situation. The bank also felt that it was urgent to provide relief to the fishing industry and that it was in line with the bank's plan, so it readily agreed and began a pilot program in the 23rd year, with an initial amount of 30,000 yuan. The Commissioner's Office organized a fishermen's lending office to be responsible for handling the matter. The county's fishing industry has always been dominated by fishing boat operations, so the loan regulations stipulate that loans should be granted to large and small fishing boats organized by fishermen, divided into three types: credit, mortgage, and guarantee. The maximum term is one year, and all loans are designated for use in fishing production. Since the loans were granted, progress has been quite good, and fishermen have been able to perform their duties, engage in production, and repay the loans on time. Last year, the loans were expanded, with the amount increased to 70,000 yuan, and the same method was used. The effect was also good. Looking at the coastal areas of Wenzhou, Taizhou, and Ningbo in Zhejiang Province, all of which are offshore fishing areas, more than 100,000 households directly or indirectly depend on fishing for a living. Therefore, the development of the fishing industry is related to the livelihoods of these more than 100,000 fishermen. At this time when the fishing industry is in danger, the scope of lending should be expanded to provide universal relief, alleviate the fishermen's difficulties, and strengthen the foundation of the fishing industry. The bank's Yuhuan fisherman loans are just a prelude.

Women's Association for Using National Goods; Expanded Recruitment

The Shanghai National Goods Movement Federation, recognizing that women preside over the family and are responsible for selecting and purchasing most household items, believes that arousing women's interest in national goods and jointly promoting their use will achieve twice the result with half the effort. Therefore, it has begun preparing to establish a Women's Association for Using National Goods. After the second Executive Committee meeting, it was decided to send letters to all members of the association and leaders of national goods factories participating in various member organizations, requesting them to invite their families to join as regular members. Following the publication of the news, many people enthusiastically joined. Warm-hearted women, driven by patriotic fervor, also came to the association to obtain membership forms and sign up. To expand public recruitment, the organization's origins, charter, and membership pledge are published below:

Origins

The origins of the organization are recorded as follows: "China has suffered foreign insults intensely, reaching its peak today. The only way to save ourselves is to restore our rights and interests by producing and using our own products and achieving self-sufficiency. Using national goods is the foundation for restoring our rights and interests. Women, as the heads of families, are responsible for purchasing clothing, food, and all kinds of utensils. Therefore, if women treat the use of national goods as a creed, economic recovery will be within easy reach. At this time when the national goods movement is extremely enthusiastic, this association, deeply mindful of the heavy responsibilities and grand aspirations of women, is initiating the Shanghai Women's Association for Using National Goods to broadly recruit like-minded individuals to strengthen our forces, gather organizations, and assist in their success. We pledge our determination and perseverance to promote this cause from one corner to the entire nation. Although the beginning is small, the results will be significant. We hope that prominent ladies and virtuous women will enthusiastically participate and lend their great names to promote this cause. We humbly present these origins for your consideration."

Charter

Article 1: Name. This association is named the Shanghai Women's Association for Using National Goods. Article 2: Purpose. This association aims to foster a habit of consistently using national goods among women through a spirit of mutual assistance and cooperation. Article 3: Members. Any woman in Shanghai or residing in Shanghai who completes a membership pledge and voluntarily joins this association, after being reviewed and registered by the association, will become a member of this association. Article 4: Staff. This association will publicly elect eleven to seventeen executive committee members at the general membership meeting to form the Executive Committee and conduct association affairs. The Executive Committee will then elect five standing committee members to form the Standing Committee and handle all daily affairs. The term of office for all positions is one year, and they may be re-elected. Article 5: Meetings. The general membership meeting will be held every six months, the Executive Committee will meet monthly, and the Standing Committee will meet every two weeks. Special meetings may be convened as needed. Article 6: Affairs. The association's affairs are defined as follows: (1) Introducing the purchase of national goods; (2) Investigating the types and quality of national goods; (3) Visiting the manufacturing of national goods; (4) Identifying the authenticity of national goods; (5) Assisting factories in promoting the sale of national goods; (6) Contacting and communicating with women's circles in various regions; (7) Assisting various regions in organizing Women's Associations for Using National Goods; (8) Going to various regions, schools, and organizations to promote and encourage the use of national goods; (9) Other matters. Article 7: Membership Fees. Members of this association are not required to pay fees, but funds may be raised temporarily when needed. Article 8: Location. The association's address is temporarily located at the Shanghai National Goods Movement Federation, Room 412, Zhonghui Bank Building, Avenue Edward VII. Article 9: Supplementary Provisions. Any matters not covered in this charter may be amended by the general membership meeting. This charter shall be officially filed with the authorities after being approved by the general membership meeting.

Pledge

The pledge reads: "I solemnly pledge to join the Shanghai Women's Association for Using National Goods as a member, abide by the association's charter, absolutely use national goods, and remain steadfast in this vow." It also records the member's name, origin, age, and address for communication.

Tea Merchants' Representatives from Foreign Firms Petition in Beijing

Requesting the Ministry of Industry's Approval to Establish a Joint Office

According to the Industry News, the Shanghai Foreign Tea Merchants Association believes that the export of Chinese tea has been affected by competition from Japan, India, and the Netherlands in recent years, leading to a decline in sales and a pessimistic outlook. To concentrate efforts and develop foreign trade, they have approved the request of their fourteen member tea firms to hold a general meeting in early this month. The meeting concluded that to revitalize tea exports, it is necessary to unite the industry and establish a joint sales office for exporting tea (including black and green tea) to unify efforts and expand overseas as much as possible. The draft charter was drafted by accountant Xu Yongzuo. It is now known that the association has sent Chairman Ye Shichang, Supervisor Sun Zifu, and consultants Yu Daxiong and Cao Yunjie, along with a petition, to Beijing on the 11 PM express train the night before last to petition the Ministry of Industry for approval to establish a unified organization for exporting tea. It is said that the representatives will return to Shanghai after obtaining satisfactory results in Beijing and begin preparations for the organization.
