China Coal Mining Industry Joint Office; Qian Zhang is Chairman and Vice-Chairman; The Regulations of the Office Have Been Approved and Implemented by the Ministry of Industry; Yesterday, Letters Were Sent to Various Industry Members Soliciting Members

According to the Shenshi News Agency, the Ministry of Industry convened a national coal mining industry conference in June of this year, which decided to establish the China Coal Mining Industry Joint Office, led by officials from the Ministry of Industry, and publicly elected Qian Xinzhi, General Manager of Zhongxing Coal Mining Company, as Chairman, and Zhang Duchen, General Manager of Lieshan Company, as Vice-Chairman at the second general meeting on the 15th of last month. They officially took office on the 14th of this month. The office moved from Foch Road to a new address on Muir Road the day before yesterday and officially began operations. As for the office's regulations, they have been approved and implemented by the Ministry of Industry with Mine Document No. 15393. Yesterday, the office sent letters to various coal mining companies soliciting members, and it is expected that participation will be enthusiastic. The charter is recorded below: Regulations of the China Coal Mining Industry Joint Office: Article 1: This office is established in accordance with the resolutions of the National Coal Mining Industry Conference convened by the Ministry of Industry on June 1, year 25 [1936], and is jointly organized by the Ministry and various coal mines, named the China Coal Mining Industry Joint Office. Article 2: The purpose of this office is to strive for the adjustment of national coal mining production and sales, the stability of its price, mutual communication, and the revitalization of industry and commerce. Article 3: This office may undertake matters related to the coal mining industry as needed, but must be resolved by the office's joint conference and submitted to the Ministry of Industry for approval. Article 4: This office is located in Shanghai and has branches in Beijing, Shanghai, Pingjin, Wuhan, Qingdao, Jinmin, Yue, and other suitable locations in the country. Article 5: All coal mines that have been approved and licensed by the Ministry may join this office as members. Each branch shall mutually elect a chairman and vice-chairman, whose terms are set for one year. Article 6: This office shall hold a joint conference once a year, and may convene temporary meetings when necessary. Article 7: Each branch is organized by responsible representatives from the related mining members in that region. Article 8: Each branch shall discuss the production and sales of bituminous coal and anthracite in groups. Article 9: Branch members shall meet once a week, and may be convened at any time when necessary. Article 10: Branch members shall submit the production and sales budgets for the first half of the year (from July of the current year) in April and the production and sales budgets for the first half of the year (from January of the next year) in October, determine the allocation of sales volume and the assessment of prices, and reach an agreement through consultation, with all members signing and acknowledging the agreement, and report it to the office, which will forward it to the Ministry of Industry for filing, to ensure compliance. Once signed, it may not be changed without the unanimous consent of all members (regarding the allocation of sales volume or the assessment of prices, if there is a dispute and no agreement can be reached, the office shall first request mediation from the China Mining Industry Federation; if mediation fails, it shall be arbitrated by the arbitration committee in item 3) (The arbitration committee shall consist of three members; in addition to inviting the Director of the Mining Department of the Ministry of Industry as a member, the other two shall be appointed by the office's general meeting with the unanimous consent of all members, with a term of five years). Article 11: If there is a violation of the agreement signed with the unanimous consent of all members as described in the above article, the branch shall report it to the office, and with the consent of four-thirds of the members present at the joint conference, it may request the Ministry of Industry to impose sanctions. Article 12: Each branch shall submit a table of monthly sales and inventory quantities and prices to the office by the beginning of the following month. The office shall compile a summary table every six months and distribute it to all members for communication. Article 13: Members of each mine in a region who wish to sell coal in other regions shall join the branch in that region as members. Article 14: If a member mine encounters force majeure or other unforeseen circumstances that hinder its business and production, it shall report the reduction in sales volume to the branch, and other member mines in the branch shall supplement it proportionally on average, and do its best to help it complete the original sales target until it returns to its original state. Article 15: Detailed rules for joint sales by each branch shall be formulated by each branch and reported to the office for filing. Article 16: Matters not covered in these regulations or amendments shall be resolved by the joint conference and reported to the Ministry of Industry for approval and filing. Article 17: These regulations shall be implemented after being approved by the Ministry of Industry.

Changshu Guild Hall Requests Correction of Abuses in Standard Measures

Merchants Have Suffered Considerable Losses Over the Years

Hoping that the Authorities Will Swiftly Crack Down

The Changshu Guild Hall sent a letter yesterday to the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs' Weights and Measures Inspection Office and the Shanghai Bean and Rice Trade Association, requesting the correction of heavy measures and obstructed scales to eliminate long-standing abuses. The letter states: "We are writing to inform you that this guild hall has found that our merchants who transport rice to Shanghai for sale do so to make a living and to adjust grain transportation and maintain food supply. However, in recent years, due to the dumping of imported rice and the unstable prices of domestic rice, our merchants have been struggling, earning very little each month. If they encounter unfortunate events such as wind and rain collisions, they suffer losses of tens of dollars for minor incidents and even lose their entire family fortune for major incidents. Compensating for losses is not enough. This shows the hardship of our merchants. Furthermore, there are long-standing inequalities among the industry members, namely that the officials cannot understand the suffering of our merchants. When transactions are completed and measures are used, heavy measures and obstructed scales are used, resulting in an average loss of 7-8 tenths to 1 liter of rice per measure for our merchants. This long-standing practice has led to endless abuses and countless harms. Over the years, they have endured hardship and cried out in vain. At this time, when the authorities are correcting measures and eliminating abuses, the government of the party and politics will surely start anew, benefiting all. We respectfully request that you swiftly crack down and correct these abuses to alleviate the merchants' difficulties and benefit their business."

Husband and Concubine Involved in Litigation Over Increased Living Expenses

Wang Gengtao Requests Severance of Relationship

Dai Xiulin Still Wishes to Cohabit

Wang Gengtao, a local resident, is 48 years old and works as a clerk in the Kaiping Coal Mining Bureau, earning a considerable income. His legal wife lives at No. 7 Shiqing Lane, Shiqing Road, Yokohama Bridge, North Sichuan Road. In the 18th year of the Republic of China [1929], Wang married Dai Xiulin (22 years old), a woman from Suzhou, as his concubine and built a separate residence at No. 2, Lane 324, Route Cardinal Foch in the French Concession. The husband and concubine had a good relationship. Wang paid Dai 35 yuan per month for expenses, rent, and food, and another 10 yuan for miscellaneous expenses. Dai saved 20 yuan, which she deposited in the Zhongfu and Guohua banks. Everything was peaceful. Recently, Dai asked Wang to increase her monthly expenses by 30 yuan to save more money for her future security. However, Wang procrastinated. Dai then hired a lawyer to send a letter to Wang for negotiation. Fearing that she would be prevented from going out, on August 5th, Dai took her clothes and savings books and went to live with relatives. Wang then hired lawyer Xu Lianghao to file a lawsuit in the Special Second Court, requesting a judgment to sever the family relationship with Dai Xiulin and recover the deposits. The defendant, Dai Xiulin, also hired lawyers Jiang Yiping and He Xiantong to file a defense and file a counterclaim, requesting the court to order the plaintiff and counterclaim defendant to increase her monthly expenses by 30 yuan. Based on the complaint, Judge Li Liang presided over the hearing in Civil Court 7 yesterday. Both parties arrived with their lawyers and stated their requests. Dai Xiulin denied running away with belongings and still wished to return home and live together. The court verified the facts and ordered the lawyers of both parties to debate before announcing the conclusion and setting the judgment for 3 PM on the 23rd before adjourning.

Shanghai Customs Notice Regarding Turning Ship Signals

Tepeke, Port Director of the Shanghai Customs (translation), issued Notice No. 14 yesterday regarding regulations for ships turning around, stating: "Upon investigation, ships in the port that wish to turn around at the corner of the Bund Park must display a special signal, as stipulated in Notice No. 13 of this department in the 12th year of the Republic of China [1923]. From October 1st of this year, ships that wish to turn around in the ship turning area shall display the following signals when approaching the area: Section 9 of this port: During the day, one black ball under a red and white triangular flag; at night, three lights, strung vertically, with the top light red and the middle and bottom lights white. Section 5 of this port (corner of the Bund Park): During the day, a red and white triangular signal flag above one black ball; at night, three lights, strung vertically, with the top and middle lights white and the bottom light red. Section 1 and upper section of this port: (A) During the day, one black ball; at night, one red and one white light, red above white. Please note that ships turning around in other sections of this port not specified in all Shanghai notices shall also display signals according to the regulations of Section 1 and upper section (A). All of the above signals must be displayed on the ship's mast or other easily visible location when approaching the turning area and may only be lowered after the turning is completed. Other ships that see these signals shall not enter the turning area until the signal is lowered. Furthermore, the signal station of the Pudong Customs will also display the signals used during the day in Sections 9 and 5 at the same time as the ships. All shipowners are hereby notified to comply."

Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Strictly Pursues Membership Fees

The City Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Association previously deliberated and approved the articles of association through a general meeting of representatives and submitted them to the Social Affairs Bureau for record. Now, it has received approval from the bureau with document number 6197. The members of the association owe a lot of membership fees, and even refuse to pay the one-time membership fee, ignoring the association itself and hindering its affairs. The association has decided at the 16th executive and supervisory meeting that for those who fail to pay membership fees, after the association's warning is ineffective, it will first file a lawsuit with the relevant court to recover the entry fee. As for the accumulated monthly fees, according to Article 20, Section 2 of the Articles of Association, "The monthly fee for a member is collected from each member's workshop based on the number of dyeing pieces in each month (1%, 2%, 3%)." The aforementioned collection standard is "regardless of any color (4% or 8% for each piece of Pǔ silk, 2% for double continuous), and 3% for all other pieces." After the end of each month, the members must report truthfully to the association within five days, and must not evade. The association will send personnel to check the dyeing registration book, verify the number of pieces, calculate the exact amount to be paid, and collect it in accordance with the regulations. If they refuse to pay, the association will pursue legal action in accordance with the Judicial Yuan's Interpretation No. 914 of the 21st year, and at the same time, in accordance with the recent central government's circular, impose penalties in accordance with the Administrative Execution Law, or request an order to suspend business.

Large Amount of Mail Seized on the He'an Steamer, Seven People Found With 156 Items, Charged with Smuggling Mail

The He'an small steamer of the China Merchants Inland River Steamer Company's Huzhou route towed a New Da Li passenger boat, a Wuxi express boat, and a silk shop boat. It arrived in Shanghai at around 7 am yesterday. The local postal authorities had received a tip-off that the chief mate and other crew members on the passenger boats were privately carrying a large number of unstamped letters from Huzhou to Shanghai for distribution and profit. Therefore, inspector Zhang Guangshu was ordered to work with customs officers Tang Yuanda and Yin Zhiyue to board a customs boat and follow the He'an steamer to the mouth of the Suzhou River when it arrived at the customs pier. They ordered the He'an to stop and boarded the boat to search. They found 16 items on the chief mate of the New Da Li, Hu Shaotang, from Shaoxing; 9 items on the New Da Li waiter, Wei Jinsheng, from Huzhou; 42 items on the New Da Li sailor, Chen Axiang, from Shaoxing; 15 items on the New Da Li waiter, Xu Jinfu, from Shaoxing; 52 items on the owner of the silk shop boat, Pan Liangui, from Huzhou; 6 items on the owner of the silk shop boat, Ru Er'er, from Shengze; and 16 items on the chief mate of the Wuxi express boat, Shen Wenlin, from Wuxi. A total of 156 items, along with two books and one folder, were seized. They were sent to the Foreign Customs Water Patrol Police Station along with the people involved. After questioning, they admitted to privately delivering mail for profit. They were charged with smuggling mail in violation of Article 2 of the National Government's Postal Regulations. Detective Hu Changqing was ordered to send the seven suspects to the local court for interrogation in the afternoon. The seized letters were handed over to postal workers for delivery after applying the appropriate postage.

Xu Yousheng Sells Drugs and Cries Loudly Upon Hearing the Sentence

Only Did it for Seven Days, Sentenced to Eight Years

Villager Regrets Committing a Crime

Xu Yousheng, a vegetable vendor from Jiangbin (35 years old), has been secretly selling heroin for profit at No. 219 Wuchang Road. This has been detected by Guo Ruiquan, a Chinese detective of the Hongkou Police Station, who sent an informant with a one-yuan legal tender bill marked secretly. The informant purchased heroin, confirming the facts. Yesterday morning at 10:50 am, they rushed to the address with a foreign detective and arrested Xu. They found 24 small packets of heroin and a marked bill in an iron can on the table, as well as copper coins from customers who had purchased drugs. They were taken to the police station for custody. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer for the Municipal Council, explained the situation and said that the defendant had stated at the police station that the drugs came from a Korean person who gave him a commission of one yuan per day. He requested a severe punishment in accordance with the law. Detective Guo then reported the details of the case and presented the drugs and the copper coins. The defendant confessed that the heroin was sent by his Korean boss every afternoon, and he sold it on his behalf. He could sell more than 20 yuan per day and had only been doing it for seven days. He claimed to be a villager who did not know that it was illegal and that he had a child and four daughters at home, pleading for leniency. Judge Zhong sentenced Xu Yousheng to eight years in prison, and the exhibits were confiscated as per the list. Xu cried loudly upon hearing the sentence and fell to the ground. The court announced that the sentence was to be carried out by shooting, which was a reduced punishment.

Malaria is Prevalent in Rural Areas, Health Centers are Finding Ways to Treat It

This year, the prevalence of mosquitoes in the suburbs of Shanghai is unprecedented in the last ten years. Merchants selling mosquito coils, mosquito incense, and other mosquito repellents are doing very well in general. Mosquitoes are the vector for malaria. In the past week, many cases of malaria have occurred in Minhang, Maqiao, Beiqiao, ZhaoJiatang, Pudong, Sanlin, Yangsi, and Chenhang. This is affecting the autumn harvest significantly. Dr. Su Delong, director of the Shanghai Suburban Health Office, has sent personnel to investigate in various villages and has prepared medicines for mass treatment. He has also sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau requesting the elimination of sewage and garbage to eliminate mosquito breeding grounds and maintain public health.

After the discovery of the bodies of a murdered man and woman buried under the floor of the Hongkou Gynecology Hospital on Zhaofeng Road, Hongkou, the Huishan Police Station took the hospital's maid Fei Wang (aka Wei Wang) into custody and sent her to the First Special District Court for detention. The strangest thing was that the uterus inside the genitals could not be found anywhere.

French Concession Rickshaws to Exchange for New Licenses

34,000 People at 20 Cents

From September, 50 Cents per Person

Exchange Licenses Starting October 1

The French Concession Public Works Department issued a notice yesterday regarding public rickshaws, stating that the Board of Directors passed a resolution on July 20, 1936, stipulating (1) the public rickshaw puller registration fee will be maintained at 20 cents per person up to 34,000 people; (2) from September 1st, the registration fee for rickshaw pullers beyond the 34,000 mark will be 50 cents per person; (3) new licenses will be exchanged from October 1st to December 31st, and the new license fee is set at 20 cents per person. The rickshaw puller armbands should be exchanged at the Vehicle Affairs Office of the French Police Station at No. 28 Xuehuali Road from October 1st of this year. The office hours are from 8 am to 12 pm and 2 pm to 5 pm daily, except Sundays. The exchange will be carried out according to the table below. All license holders must comply with the following deadlines: October 1st to 3rd, numbers 1 to 1,500; 5th to 10th, numbers 1,501 to 4,500; 12th to 17th, numbers 4,501 to 7,500; 19th to 24th, numbers 7,501 to 10,500; October 26th to 31st, numbers 10,501 to 13,500; November 2nd to 7th, numbers 13,501 to 16,500; 9th to 14th, numbers 16,501 to 19,500; 16th to 21st, numbers 19,505 to 22,500; 23rd to 28th, numbers 22,501 to 25,500; November 30th to December 5th, numbers 25,501 to 28,500; 7th to 12th, numbers 28,501 to 31,500; 14th to 19th, numbers 31,501 to 34,000. All rickshaw pullers must exchange their licenses and armbands within the specified period. Those who fail to do so by the deadline risk having their rickshaw licenses revoked. Take note.

Liuhai Sandbar Outside Wusongkou, the Sandspit Suddenly Expands, the Hydrographic Office Issues a Notice, Warning Navigators to Pay Attention

The sandspit on the north bank of Liuhai Sandbar, located at the mouth of the Yangtze River outside Wusongkou, has suddenly expanded. The local Hydrographic Office issued Notice No. 211 yesterday, warning that the direction, orientation, and distance of the expanded sandspit on the north bank of Liuhai Sandbar from the Liuhai Sandbar Beacon are (A) 337 degrees 2.94 nautical miles, (B) 330 degrees 3.24 nautical miles, (C) 326 degrees 3.68 nautical miles, with a depth of 28 feet (8.53 meters), 29 feet (8.84 meters), and 29 feet (8.84 meters). The longitude is 120 degrees 43 minutes east, and the latitude is approximately 32 degrees 0 minutes north. Explanation: The above depths of A, B, and C all refer to the water depth on the northern edge of the Liuhai Sandbar sandspit.

Liu A'bing Obstructs Official Business: Admits to Throwing Lime, Denies Chopping with Ax; Court Police Officer Sun Provides Detailed Account of Injury; Debate Concludes, Sentencing on the 23rd

A row of houses at No. 162 Changping Road in West Shanghai is the property of a local man named Shen. Because several tenants owed rent for months, Shen filed a lawsuit in the civil court of the First Special District Court. A judgment was made for the tenants to repay the full amount. When the execution date arrived on the 15th of last month, the court dispatched clerk Yang Yumin, bailiff Lu Zhaoxiong, and judicial police officer No. 12 Sun Qingshan to seize the property. Unexpectedly, when they arrived at the door of No. 148 for execution, Liu A'bing (age 54) from Jiangyin, a resident of the house, resisted. He threw lime at bailiff Lu and police officer Sun. He also used an ax to chop officer Sun four times, causing severe injuries. The police were alerted and dispatched detectives who transported officer Sun to the Municipal Council Hospital for treatment. Simultaneously, the assailant Liu A'bing, along with the ax, were taken into custody by the First Special District Court. Because officer Sun's injuries had not healed, Liu was ordered to be detained pending interrogation. Details of this event have been previously reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that officer Sun's injuries have slightly improved. This morning, the police escorted Liu A'bing to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Special District Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin prosecuted him for obstructing official duties under Articles 135, Section 132 of the Criminal Code. According to the victim, officer No. 12 Sun Qingshan, on the morning of August 15th, he was ordered to accompany clerk Yang, bailiff Lu, and others to Changping Road for seizure. Four houses had already been completed. The defendant was the fifth house. Unexpectedly, upon seeing them, the defendant immediately questioned bailiff Lu about why he had not been notified before sealing the door, leading to an argument. The defendant first threw lime at Lu. When Sun stepped forward to intervene, the defendant took lime from his pocket and threw it at him. At that time, while Sun was bending down to pick up a fallen seal, the defendant picked up more lime from the wall and threw it, then fiercely chopped at him four times with the ax, blinding his eyes. His waist, back, and legs were severely injured. Subsequently, the police transported him to the Municipal Council Hospital. At the time, his body was swollen, his breathing was rapid, and his life was in grave danger. Fortunately, President Xie and Doctor Guo provided emergency treatment and dedicated care, preserving his life. However, he has not fully recovered and requests severe punishment. When questioned, the defendant admitted to throwing lime twice, but denied chopping with the ax four times. He claimed that because he was surrounded, he simply threw a wood-splitting knife, which happened to hit the officer. After debate by both lawyers, Judge Huang announced that the case would be sentenced on the 23rd, and the defendant was returned to police custody.

Educational Circle Personnel Sue for Daughter

Chen Jingchu and He Chengfu Fall Out

Incorrect Jurisdiction, Awaiting Transfer for Handling

Chen Jingchu, a native of Yancheng residing at No. 36 Huangjia Que Road, outside the West Gate of the Chinese-controlled area, serving as an inspector in the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, after his wife, Wu, passed away on July 8th of last year, adopted his three-year-old daughter, Xiaofeng, to He Chengfu, a classmate from Zhuji residing at No. 66 Ruihua Fang, Route Lafayette, in the French Concession, who serves as the director of academic affairs at Minli Girls' Middle School and concurrently as the head of Qingxin Girls' School. Recently, Chen suddenly wanted to reclaim his daughter, but after unsuccessful negotiations, Chen reported to the French police station, accusing He Chengfu and his wife, He Qiu, of enticing away the girl. The French Police Department transferred the case to the Second Special District Court, initiating a public prosecution under Article 241 of the Criminal Code. After questioning by Judge Zhang Chaozuo, the hearing was postponed and both parties were instructed to reconcile outside of court, as previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Judge Zhang again summoned them in the First Criminal Court, asking if the two parties had made any progress in reconciliation outside of court. According to He Chengfu, yesterday, Education Bureau specialist Jiang Wenbao and Sun Bawu came to his school and tried to reconcile with the principal. Because he was groundlessly accused and his reputation was affected, the plaintiff's accusation of enticing was not supported by evidence. Regarding the extortion point, he was not thinking about money. If the other party could issue a public apology in the newspapers, compensating him for his fostering losses, he could reconcile and return the child. Last night, Jiang came to his house, but he was out. Jiang left a business card, asking him to come to court today, but the situation changed again. Plaintiff Chen Jingchu claimed that He was demanding a large sum of money, forcing him to resort to the law. If He wanted him to apologize, he would respect the law, and if he was wrong, he would accept legal punishment. Subsequently, mediators Wang Manyun and Sun Bawu, two lawyers, arrived to mediate. Both parties agreed on the point of returning fostering losses, with Chen compensating He 300 yuan. However, plaintiff Chen Jingchu absolutely refused to apologize. Defendant He Chengfu insisted that reconciliation was impossible without an apology. After a long period, reconciliation ultimately failed. The court, seeing that both parties were tending towards extremes and both wanted to reclaim the child, declared the reconciliation broken and ordered the debate to begin. Police Department lawyer Yuan Jiahua argued that according to the plaintiff's report to the police station, the defendant's wife went to the plaintiff's residence and took the child away. The location of the incident was in the Chinese-controlled area, and according to Article 4 of the agreement, it was not under the jurisdiction of the court and should be handled according to the law. After further debate by the defendant's lawyer, the court declared the conclusion. The court ruled that the case was under incorrect jurisdiction and would be transferred to the Jiangsu Shanghai Local Court for trial. Chen Xiaofeng would be temporarily sent to a nursery for care. Both parties were ordered to pay 50 yuan each to the court.

The Tang Couple Sues the Labor Hospital: Where Did the White Powder Come From? Changes Charge From Negligent Homicide to Injury; Court Orders Zhang Xiuyu to Be Summoned for Further Questioning

Tang Liwen, a native of Zhenjiang residing at No. 450, Lane 391, Jiangjia Lane, Route Gordon, and his wife, Tang Wang, recently hired lawyer Tao Gan to sue the doctor of the Labor Hospital at No. 1000 Xiaoshadu Road in the First Special District Court for attempted negligent homicide. The gist of the lawsuit is roughly as follows: The plaintiff's one-year-old son, Da Shizi, was suffering from dysentery in late August of this year. On the afternoon of the 4th of this month at 2:00 PM, they went to the Labor Hospital for diagnosis. The doctor prescribed six packets of white powder, instructing them to administer one packet every hour, mixed with boiled water. The plaintiff administered one packet to Da Shizi at 5:00 PM, but the child refused to eat it. As soon as the medicine entered his mouth, he spat it out. Unexpectedly, wherever the ejected medicine landed, the skin and flesh corroded instantly, and blisters and swelling appeared in his mouth. His throat became painful and changed color immediately. They immediately inquired at the hospital, but the doctor did not admit to prescribing the wrong medicine and took away three packets of the prescribed powder, leaving only one packet. At 9:00 PM that night, they reported to the Putuo Road police station, which dispatched detectives for investigation. The doctor's name was not disclosed, and the child's condition was severe. They were immediately sent to Baolong Hospital, where the hospital's doctor confirmed that the powder was poisonous. Therefore, they are filing a lawsuit under Articles 276, Section 2 and 271, Section 2 of the Criminal Code and request the retrieval of records to verify the doctor's name. The court, noting that there is no such crime as attempted negligent homicide under the Criminal Code, summoned the plaintiff alone yesterday afternoon. The investigating judge opened the Eighth Criminal Court to hear the case and informed the plaintiff of the situation, also showing the police station's files for review. It was then learned that the attending doctor was Zhang Xiuyu (female). The plaintiff's lawyer immediately requested a change in the article of law, prosecuting for negligent injury under Article 284, Section 2 of the Criminal Code. The court ordered the date to be changed to the afternoon of the 25th to summon Zhang Xiuyu for further questioning.

Former Detective Zhao Jinquan: False Accusation of Judges' Interrogation Record; Misunderstanding of New and Old Cases; Results in Bribery Rumor Case

Zhao Jinquan, a former detective of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, arrested two pickpockets, Geng Zhongyi and others, at Xinqiao, west of Xiejiao. The police chief in charge, Zhang Dasi, considered his arrest to be rash and detained Zhao Jinquan and Geng Zhongyi together at the substation. Patrol Officer Nie Shaowen ordered Zhao and others to be handcuffed and sent to the Ximen Sub-bureau before sending them to the Public Security Bureau. The handcuffs were then removed from Zhao. The Public Security Bureau handed Geng Zhongyi and others over to the local court for trial and sentencing to three months' imprisonment. Zhao Jinquan then accused Nie Shaowen, Zhang Dasi, and others of injury to the local court. The prosecutor ordered Nie Shaowen and Zhang Dasi to appear in court for interrogation.

A letter from Li Jing, former director of the Ximen Sub-bureau,

guaranteed their release. However, when the public prosecution was initiated, Nie and Zhang failed to appear. The case was not concluded. Details were reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that Zhao Jinquan felt resentful because, although Li Jing had resigned, he should still be responsible for ensuring Nie and Zhang's appearance. He repeatedly filed petitions requesting a thorough investigation. Recently, Zhao Jinquan again accused Li Jing of bribing judges. After receiving the accusation, the court ordered Zhao Jinquan to appear in court. Prosecutor Lei Binzhang interrogated and detained him, believing that Zhao Jinquan had indeed made a false accusation and filed

a public prosecution according to the law.

It was briefly stated that Zhao Jinquan, formerly a detective of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, was interfered with by police chief and patrol officer Nie Shaowen of the Ximen Sub-bureau on June 3rd of last year while arresting thieves. He had previously investigated and accused Nie Shaowen and others of injury. During the investigation, Nie Shaowen and others were released on guarantee by Li Jing, director of the Xidou Sub-bureau. They failed to appear during the trial. Zhao Jinquan requested Judge He Jingcen to sign an arrest warrant for Li Jing, which was approved and requested by the Shanghai Second Special District Court for assistance in the arrest, but was not successful. Zhao Jinquan then filed a complaint against Li Jing for facilitating escape, with the complaint marked as Case No. 2287 of the Litigation Department of the 24th year, the number of a previously submitted old case. He instructed the receiver's office to submit it to the court's dispatch office. However, Zhu Binglin, who submitted the complaint on his behalf, did not declare that it was a new case. He took the complaint back and had Zhao Jinquan rewrite it, which he

submitted by post.

Prosecutor Kong Xianglin sent a letter to the Shanghai Second Special District Court requesting assistance in summoning Li Jing for investigation and decided not to prosecute. A request for reconsideration was filed and was rejected by the Chief Prosecutor of the Jiangsu High Court. Zhao Jinquan then added fabricated facts, claiming that Judge He refused to arrest Li Jing, the receiving office refused to accept his complaint against Li Jing, and Prosecutor Kong did not detain Li Jing when he appeared in court and did not believe that Li Jing had appeared in court. On November 24th of last year, he saw Li Jing, who claimed that he had sent 5,000 yuan to Judge He, rendering your lawsuit ineffective, and that Feng Guming could testify to this. He filed a complaint with the court accusing Judge He and Prosecutor Kong of dereliction of duty and accepting bribes. After thorough investigation, based on the following evidence, it was determined that Zhao Jinquan was suspected of

false accusation

and should be prosecuted according to the law. The evidence and his criminal articles are as follows: Zhao Jinquan accused Judge He Jingcen and Prosecutor Kong Xianglin of dereliction of duty and accepting bribes, solely based on seeing Li Jing moving on November 14th of last year in Dajili. He went up to question him about whether he would appear in court on the 18th. Li replied that whether he appeared or not was irrelevant because he had already sent 5,000 yuan in banknotes to Judge He of the local court, rendering your lawsuit ineffective. Feng Guming was beside him and heard Li Jing say this. However, when Feng Guming was questioned, he

claimed he did not hear this. Li Jing originally lived at No. 4, Dajili, Fangxie Road, and vacated the premises on October 17th of last year. Tenant Chen Xinmeng was summoned and presented the rental record book, which was verified. According to

Chen Xinmeng's testimony,

they gave him a few days of rent, and he moved out around the end of October, definitely not in November. Therefore, Zhao Jinquan's claim that he saw Li Jing moving on November 14th of last year is completely false. Since Li Jing had already moved, claiming that he saw Li Jing moving in Dajili on November 14th of last year and claiming that there was bribery is a fabricated fact and a deliberate false accusation, which is undoubtedly beyond doubt. The defendant has indeed committed the crime under Article 169, Section 1 of the Criminal Code. Yesterday morning, Judge Chen Kangsun

opened the court for trial.

Zhao Jinquan, who was in custody, was brought to the case. He stated that he was 36 years old, from Gaoyou, residing on Liyuan Road, and formerly a detective of the Municipal Public Security Bureau. He was asked why he accused the court staff. He replied that on November 14th of last year, he saw Li Jing sitting on a moving truck, so he asked him if he was going to court on the 18th. Li replied that it didn't matter whether he went or not because he had already sent 5,000 yuan to the judge. He was asked why he accused Prosecutor Kong. He replied that it was because the complaint could not be delivered, so he sent it to Chief Zhong by mail, which was to accuse Li Jing of

facilitating escape.

Because the court said that Li Jing had been acquitted, he was asked not to recklessly make false accusations. Even if he refused to appear, he could not immediately say it was bribery. Moreover, in your statement to the prosecutor's office, the statement that Li Jing bribed 5,000 yuan was heard by witness Feng Guming, but when questioned, Feng Guming denied it, which shows that you are falsely accusing. At this point, witness Feng Guming was brought to the case. He stated that he was 34 years old, from Dongtai, and practiced traditional Chinese medicine. In October of last year, he was passing through the intersection of Dajili and Fangxie Road when he saw Zhao Jinquan in conflict with someone wearing a suit. He only heard the person wearing the suit say, "You can sue me if you want, I

have money ready

to fight the lawsuit." As for the 5,000 yuan, he did not hear it. However, there were indeed moving trucks nearby. Witness Wang Guiliang stated that he was the doorman in Dajili and that Li Jing used to live at No. 4 in the lane. He hired a moving truck around the end of October. He was asked if he had seen Li Jing in conflict with anyone, and he replied that he did not know. Lawyer Li Ming, who was retained by the defendant, stated that Li Jing did move by truck and requested that the court investigate the exact date of Li Jing's move. The judge then ordered Zhao Jinquan to be returned to custody pending further notice.

Western Paint Industry Guild: Sues for Embezzlement Before Examining Accounts; Difficult to Be a Director of the Group; Allegations of the Plaintiff Are Empty

Because major merchants Le Zhenbao, Bei Runsheng, Zhang Lanping, Le Gengrong, and others serve as directors of the Foreign Goods Commercial Guild, they were previously sued by the Shanghai Western Paint Industry Guild, with Ma Shangjie as their agent, in the Second Special District Court. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Chen Shuoying visited the Second Court to summon both parties for continued trial. Both sides arrived with their respective lawyers. First, Li Zuyu, the defense lawyer for the defendants, stated to the court that the plaintiff's side initially filed the lawsuit in the name of the guild, but later listed the names of ten merchant firms of the plaintiffs in the application. He questioned whether they could file a lawsuit and whether the merchant firms had the capacity to act. He asked the court to pay attention to this. He further stated that the self-proclaimed agent Ma Shangjie was the representative of ten firms, which raised issues under the Criminal Procedure Law. The court said that the plaintiff had submitted a petition today. Lin Yingqing, the defense lawyer for Le Zhenbao, stated that Precedent No. 533 of the Supreme Court in the 20th year of the Republic stated that merchant firms did not have the capacity to act and could not file a lawsuit. The court pointed out that the power of attorney from the plaintiff's side authorized Ma Shangjie, Zhang Shizhao, Chao Kun, Gao Danhua, He Xiaoyuan, etc., which was illegal. Ma replied that Zhang Shizhao had given up and was not appearing in court. The judge stated that four agents were also illegal. Ma replied that nine plaintiffs had authorized him as their representative and had hired three lawyers. At this point, the defendants' lawyer asked the court to resolve the procedural issues first. The court immediately summoned defendant Le Zhenbao for questioning, ordering him to present the three pieces of evidence he had been ordered to bring. Le replied that he had brought them. Zhang Lanping presented the deed of ownership, title deed, and minutes of the meeting. He also presented two bankbooks for the Foreign Goods Commercial Guild and the Renyi Shan Hui from the 23rd and 24th years. Le Zhenbao was asked if the general meeting recorded in the minutes was the same one as on September 22nd of the 23rd year. He replied that it was. Because the Foreign Goods Commercial Guild was illegal and could not be registered, it was reorganized into Renyi Shan Hui. He was a director and did not ask about the accounts of the association. Lin Binyi had previously served as the clerk, and after Lin died this year, someone else took over collecting rent, and someone else managed the association. He was asked if the plaintiff now requested to examine the accounts. He replied that the accounts were in the association and managed by the clerk. Li Zuyu, the defendant's lawyer, stated that regarding the plaintiff's accusation of embezzlement, the plaintiff should point out the facts before the court ordered an investigation of the accounts. Moreover, defendant Le Zhenbao was a director and did not ask about the accounts. Bei Runsheng was asked if he attended the reorganization of Renyi Shan Hui. He replied that he did not attend, but there was a signature book. He resigned as director and sent a letter of notification before it was published in the newspaper. Zhang Lanping was asked if he knew about the bank transactions. He replied that he did not know. He was a director and had many things to do himself. Unless there was a meeting, he would not go to the association. Le Gengrong was asked if he knew about the association's accounts. He replied that he did not manage them. The association was established in the 32nd year of Guangxu, and he was only 19 years old at that time. At this point, the plaintiff Ding Fang'e was summoned, but did not arrive. A representative was sent, but the court did not question them. Shen Leshan was summoned and stated that he was the assistant manager of Wanshunge, acting as manager. The firm had donated money, but the receipt had been lost for many years. Defendant Lin Yingqing, after Shen Leshan's statement, stated to the court that Wanshunge had closed down and Shen was not the manager of Wanshunge. He was now working for Bu Nei Men Foreign Firm and could not come to court to represent Wanshunge. The plaintiff Chen Gengsheng was summoned and stated that various friends in the store had donated money, but the receipt had been lost. The plaintiff Li Shuyan was summoned and stated that he did not participate in the lawsuit. Although his name was listed on the complaint, he did not sign it. Finally, the court asked the plaintiff's representative, Ma Shangjie, how the defendants embezzled funds. Ma replied that their accounts had never been public, which constituted fraud. Defendant Yan Yinwu's lawyer stated that the subject of the lawsuit had not been determined, and the plaintiff's claims were even more empty. Lawyer Lin Yingqing stated that the plaintiff was now discussing property issues in court, but during previous mediation, they had only sought 300 yuan in subsidies. As a result, the court ordered the case to be adjourned to 2:00 PM on the 25th for further questioning and ordered the defendants to submit the account books of the Foreign Goods Commercial Guild for verification.

They are currently seeking a suitable large building as the association's headquarters. The formal establishment date is imminent. This is also good news for the natives of Songjiang residing in Shanghai.

Wuzhou Pharmacy Plans to Manufacture Arsenic Organic Synthetics

Since the establishment of the second factory, Shanghai Wuzhou Pharmacy has produced a variety of organic synthetic drugs, which have been sold on the market and have been praised by the medical community. Recently, they have been researching arsenic organic compounds (Salvarsan type, used to treat syphilis), and they have more than ten experimental products. They will invite pharmacology experts to conduct precise tests to determine which is the most effective. It is reported that satisfactory results have been achieved, and large-scale manufacturing is planned soon. This is not only good news for patients in our country, but also an important plan to recover rights.

Yongchuan Hospital Opens Tomorrow

Yongchuan Hospital has a history of more than ten years and has saved countless lives. Director Wang Zhenchuan, to develop his business, moved to a newly built building opposite the Empire Theatre in Bazi Bridge, French Concession, last month. After two months of equipment installation, the electrotherapy equipment, operating room, wards, etc. have been completed. It will open on the 20th of this month, with light refreshments prepared to welcome guests to visit. The hospital's departments include internal medicine, surgery, obstetrics and gynecology, pediatrics, venereal disease, and smoking cessation. The consultation fee is low, based on the principle of making it economical for the common people. The poor are treated free of charge and given medicine, which is truly a blessing to society.

The Shanghai Lawyer's Association, in preparation for the construction of a new clubhouse, will soon commence work on demolishing its existing clubhouse at 572 Beile Road. Second Special District National Exhibition Extends Display for Two Weeks

Notification to Manufacturers to Re-register

The Second Special District National Exhibition, located at the intersection of Avenue Petain and Xujiahui in this city, has been open for a month. The temporary market and amusement park attached to the exhibition have been extremely crowded daily, with total business revenue exceeding 36,000 yuan, an excellent result that surpasses the records of previous national exhibitions. The exhibition was originally scheduled to close tonight. However, due to requests from manufacturers to extend the exhibition period, it was decided at yesterday's meeting to approve a two-week extension. Simultaneously, manufacturers are being notified to re-register. The notification states: "Regarding the matter of notification, the exhibition has been open until now and is about to expire. As it is now autumn, the time for autumn goods to enter the market, and the number of visitors will inevitably be large, manufacturers who have not yet participated in the exhibition have requested an extension of the exhibition period. For this reason, the exhibition has approved a two-week extension and will re-organize and decorate the interior to enhance its appearance. It has been decided that each department will subsidize room and electricity fees, totaling seven yuan per room. Those who wish to participate must register with the exhibition office immediately. In order to provide preferential treatment, those who register first will be given priority to avoid missing out due to full capacity. This is a special notification."

City News

Norwegian Cod Liver Oil Sells Well Every Autumn season is the time when cod liver oil enters the market. Because it contains Vitamins A and D, it is most effective in preventing coughs and other diseases. However, cod liver is a natural specialty of Norway, so the Norwegian government monitors its production to ensure its purity and sufficient quantity. Therefore, it sells well worldwide, and sales in Shanghai are also quite considerable.

Yiyuan Company's Low-Price Promotion Attracts Crowds Yiyuan Company, located at Dongxin Bridge in the Public Concession, is issuing high-quality white fungus, ginseng bird's nest, and famous Sichuan local products, as well as various gift items. The quality of the goods is excellent, and the prices are fair, which has always been praised by the public. Therefore, its business is thriving, with a significant leap forward. To commemorate its eighth anniversary, the company is holding a major price reduction and offering many "sacrifice items" and "buy-one-get-one-free" goods to attract customers. In recent days, door-to-door sales and mail orders have been exceptionally enthusiastic, creating a scene of being overwhelmed with customers like on Shanyin Road.

Yuanchang Hardware Store News Yuanchang Hardware Store, located at the corner of Guizhou Road and Ningbo Road, specializes in window curtains, carpets, and other decorations for hotels, theaters, homes, and offices. Since its establishment, it has adhered to the business principle of small profits and quick turnover, earning a considerable reputation. Recently, feeling that the space is insufficient for its needs, it has expanded its store to facilitate business. It has also lowered the prices of all goods and has been appointed as the general agent by Ames Company. Therefore, orders from both local and out-of-town customers are pouring in.

Nanyang Soap and Candle Factory Offers Big Promotions Nanyang Soap and Candle Factory, located at the north end of Old Rubbish Bridge, has been established for over twenty years and enjoys a long-standing reputation. Due to renovations at its original site, it has moved its office to North Zhejiang Road. Now that the renovations are complete, it has moved back to its original site and resumed business as usual. To reward customers, it held a special "buy-one-get-one-free" promotion on the opening day, and starting yesterday, it will continue to offer big promotions for fourteen days.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: The atmosphere in and around Shandong and the Yellow River basin is clear and cool, with cloudy conditions in several places and southwest to northwest winds. The upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River have gentle winds with no fixed direction. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River, the East Sea, and Taiwan all have northeast winds and morning fog. There is a low-pressure area in the Pacific Ocean. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 83.5 degrees, and the lowest was 68.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 81.5 degrees, and the lowest was 61.2 degrees.

Sports News

European Travel Diary

— Li Huitang, from London

(August 11) Lately, I have been watching sports and visiting famous scenic spots, and I do not feel the pain of boredom. After our team's failure in the Games, newspapers and commentators have given us excellent reviews. Therefore, various European countries have sent letters inviting us. For the sake of observing and learning more, although we know that victory is hopeless, we are happy to receive instruction. So, our team did not wait for the closing of the Games and left Berlin by train at 9:00 this morning, arriving in Frankfurt, southern Germany, at 5:00. This city is a famous historical site and the industrial hub of Germany. The Da Xu Berlin also has a station here. In the evening, we were invited to watch an open-air theater performance, which was quite eye-opening. According to my impressions of this Games, although they are very vague, based on my observations, all sports have progressed by ten feet, while we have only progressed by one foot. If we do not fundamentally find a way to innovate, we will never be able to catch up to the standards. I hope that our country's sports authorities will learn a lesson from this and do something to improve.

(August 12) Today we were supposed to compete with a selected team from Southern Germany, but the weather was not good, with heavy rain, so we had to postpone the game. Tomorrow morning, we will be welcomed by the city government and presented with gifts, which I will acknowledge. Then, we will visit various places in the city and the Chinese Academy of Culture, which houses Chinese books, antiques, and cultural wedding dramas, clothing, music, etiquette, everything you could want. Abroad (August 14) We left Germany at 7:00 in the morning by train to Vienna, the capital of Austria, arriving at nightfall. Austrian football players are salaried, and their strength is the best in Europe. Last year, a British professional team came to compete with them and returned defeated. Their strength can be imagined.

(August 15) In the morning, we took a special trip to tour the area. There are many historical sites in this city, which are quite interesting. In the afternoon, we competed with the runner-up team and were defeated by a score of four to two. However, this result is worth celebrating. Austrian football techniques follow the Scottish style, using a lot of triangular short passes for attacks. Although we lost today, we learned many good points.

(August 16) Yesterday, I received news from the Games that Italy finally won the World Cup football championship. I was very envious upon hearing this. In the morning, Director Rong arrived from Berlin to join us. In the afternoon, we met with a strong professional champion team and were miserably defeated by a score of twelve to zero. I have never experienced such a defeat in my life, and I am truly ashamed. The main reasons for our great defeat were: first, we had neglected training after our defeat at the Games; second, we had been traveling by train and in battle too frequently in recent days, resulting in many injuries on the field, and we only had nine players to compete; third, the whole team's morale was scattered, and we were no longer as united as we were during the Southern tour. There were quarrels on the field at every turn. Today, Feng Bao even fought each other out of anger, which was a great loss of civility and the purpose of sports. This great lesson may be a stimulant for the development of football in our country.

(August 17) After the great defeat today, we took a short rest. In the afternoon, we attended a tea party hosted by Minister Liu Chongjie.

(August 18) Early in the morning, we were on the road again, taking a train to Switzerland. There were many tunnels along the way, and the scenery was beautiful, so we did not feel the journey was difficult. We arrived in Bern in the evening and stayed for one night. Here, we met the Japanese football team, who will show their skills here tomorrow.

(August 19) After a brief tour in the morning, we continued our journey by train, arriving in Geneva, the world-renowned city of peace, in the evening. This is where the League of Nations meets. It has mountains and lakes, and its beauty does not yield to West Lake, and the climate is warm and pleasant. People say that Switzerland's scenery is the best in the world, and it is not an exaggeration.

(August 20) After breakfast, we took a special car and asked a guide to take us to see the sights. It was very interesting to listen to their explanations. Reading the newspaper, the Japanese team was defeated by a score of sixteen to one in Zurich, which shows the strength of Swiss football. Fortunately, we cheered up today and worked hard, and we won by a score of three to two. I personally scored three goals, and defender Dasheng performed the best. It was a rare and commendable victory in our European tour. We were treated to a feast by the local overseas Chinese, and we dispersed happily.

(August 21) At 9:00, we heard the sound of wheels again, heading towards Paris. We had been traveling and racing every day, and we were too tired. As soon as the car started, all the members were dreaming in their bunks, looking haggard, truly a pitiful team. We arrived in Paris at 6:30 in the afternoon. Those who welcomed us at the station included the ambassador's representative, the French government's sports minister, and many people from the overseas Chinese community. It was very lively and touching. Paris is the world's most romantic city, with a sea of ​​desire and a flesh market. The city is open all night, and its licentiousness is even more rampant than other cities in Europe. I had heard people say this before, but I did not dare to believe it. Now that I have seen it with my own eyes, I know that there is such a strange situation in the world.

(August 22) French professional football started four years ago, and most of the top players are hired from abroad. Its strength is quite strong. Today, we competed against them and performed wonderfully, resulting in a tie of two to two, which is also a good result. After the game, people from the French football club even asked me if I was interested in staying in France to play football, saying that they would offer me a signing bonus of 30,000 francs and a monthly salary of 2,500 francs. I declined with a smile because I am getting older and will soon retire. However, it is a happy thing that my football skills have attracted the attention of the professional world.

(August 23) Last night, I suddenly suffered from diarrhea. This morning, our team left for Le Havre, France, to compete. I could not accompany them due to my illness. Afterwards, I heard that everyone performed very poorly and was defeated by a score of six to zero. My absence must have had a significant impact.

(August 24) In the morning, I went to buy an airplane ticket because I will be flying to Sweden tomorrow to visit industrial and commercial enterprises. In the afternoon, I attended a tea party hosted by the embassy. In the evening, I went with a friend to watch nude dancing, which was bizarre and colorful, opening my eyes to a new world. Even someone who is indifferent to this would open their eyes wide.

(August 25) At 7:00 in the morning, I took a plane to Stockholm, the capital of Sweden, because I work for a Swedish trading company and had to take some time to visit the head office and investigate the industry and commerce. The plane flew for eight hours before safely arriving at its destination. Along the way, we passed through Belgium, Germany, Denmark, and other places. Overlooking Europe, it was particularly interesting. Sweden is celebrating peace everywhere. Everyone lives and works in peace, like in a peach blossom garden, which is completely different from Paris.

(August 29) In recent days, I have traveled around Sweden, visiting famous cities and scenic spots, and visiting many industrial and commercial enterprises, which has increased my knowledge a lot. I have been very popular everywhere. Every time I arrive at a place, my photos are published in the newspapers, and it is considered a great regret that our team could not come to Sweden to compete. Today, I started my return journey to London from Gothenburg (Swedish coast). While passing through the capital of the Netherlands, a flight attendant told me that our team had lost to them in a light battle the previous night by a score of five to three. At 5:00 in the afternoon, I safely arrived in London. London is the world's largest city, with a vast area and a population of eight million. The traffic is complicated. Our team had already arrived here from the Dutch capital last night. Today, we were invited to visit a professional football game. Unfortunately, when I arrived at the stadium, the game was over. Fortunately, I was able to shake hands with Mr. James and others in the changing room, fulfilling a lifelong wish, which made me very happy. After reuniting with my comrades, I was invited to visit the night scenery in the South City, which I found quite interesting. There will be two games here, both against the amateur champion team, the results of which will be reported later. Also, our team will leave London for Italy early on September 2nd and take the Conte Rosso on the 4th to return to China. We should arrive in Hong Kong by September 24th. (September 2nd) On August 31st, we narrowly lost to the Corinthians team by a score of two to three, earning unlimited praise. Ji Liang and I were the most popular. On September 1st, we lost to the Casuals team again by a score of two to five. Our football games have now come to an end. We are preparing to go to Italy today and take a boat to return home.

Municipal Sports Field Open Soccer Regulations

Starting October 5th

The regulations for the first Municipal Sports Field Open Soccer Tournament are as follows:

(1) Purpose: To promote sports and popularize soccer.

(2) Tournament Date: Starting October 5th.

(3) Registration: From September 20th to September 30th.

(4) Registration Procedure: When registering, a registration form must be submitted, along with a registration fee of two yuan (non-refundable) and a six-inch photo of all players. The numbers must be filled in for verification. Those who do not have a group photo may supplement it with a recent personal photo. Those who have a name on the registration form but no photo, or those who have a photo but are not registered, will not be allowed to participate in the competition.

(5) Registration Location: Guidance Group Office, Municipal Sports Field, City Center District.

(6) This tournament will use a single round-robin system.

(7) The competing teams must arrive at the field ten minutes before the game. If they do not arrive at the field within the specified time, they will be deemed to have forfeited.

(8) If a competing team cannot attend a game due to special circumstances, it must contact the Committee in writing one day in advance. No temporary requests for rescheduling will be accepted.

(9) Those who withdraw or are disqualified midway through the tournament will have their results cancelled and not counted.

(10) Each team must not participate in two tournaments. Violators will be disqualified from the tournament.

(11) The clothing of each participating team must be uniform for identification.

(12) If there is a protest, a formal written statement must be submitted to the Committee within 24 hours after the incident. The decision of the adjudication committee shall be final and no further protests will be allowed. (A protest deposit of five yuan in national currency must be paid for each protest. If the protest is successful, it will be refunded afterwards; otherwise, it will be confiscated.)

(13) The game ball will be provided by this field.

(14) All game locations will be at this field.

(15) Referees will be assigned or hired by the Guidance Group of this field.

(16) The order and date of the games will be determined by this field and notified separately.

(17) Whether the game will be postponed due to rain can be inquired from this office.

(18) Any imperfections in these regulations may be amended by the Committee.

Shanghai Universities Tennis Championship Regulations Starting October 3rd

The regulations for the Shanghai Universities Tennis Championship are as follows:

(1) Name: Shanghai Universities Tennis Championship.

(2) Purpose: To develop sports, increase interest in tennis, and connect the feelings of universities.

(3) Organization: Organized by the Shanghai Universities Sports Association.

(4) Competition: The competition includes three groups of singles and two groups of doubles. The team that wins three groups is the winner. The knockout system will be used to determine the championship.

(5) Competition Venue: Tennis court at the Municipal Sports Field in the city center, with centralized competition.

(6) Start Date: Starting October 13th.

(7) Registration Date: From September 20th to September 27th.

(8) Registration Procedure: The sports department of each school shall prepare a registration form, indicating the first singles, second singles, third singles, first doubles, second doubles, and reserve members, signed by the sports director, and submit it along with a registration fee of five yuan to the association's resident tennis committee member, Wang Fudan. New members must also pay a membership fee of twenty yuan.

(9) Player Qualifications: Regardless of new or old members, students who have been studying at the school for more than one year are eligible to represent the school.

(10) Ball: Slazenger Cho brand will be used, and each of the two schools competing will be responsible for half of the cost.

(11) Rules: The 24th National Games tennis rules will be adopted.

(12) Spectators: There is no fee to watch the game, but the rules must be followed.

Shanghai Jiaotong University Sports Association Held a Basketball Representatives Meeting Yesterday

Competition Begins on the 4th of Next Month

The Sports Federation of Various Agencies of the Ministry of Communications in Shanghai held a meeting of representatives of various teams in the first basketball competition yesterday at the Federation's clubhouse. More than ten representatives from member postal remittance offices, Eurasia Airlines, telephone bureaus, international radio stations, China Merchants Bureau, China Aviation Corporation, postal bureaus, and telegraph bureaus attended. Xu Duo, director of the competition department of the Federation, chaired the meeting. The resolutions are recorded as follows: (1) The opening date is set for the 4th of next month. The roster of each team must be submitted to the Federation before the 30th of this month. (2) The competition will adopt a single round-robin system, and the balls will be provided by the Federation. (3) The competition rules will adopt the latest basketball rules approved by the China National Sports Federation. (4) The competition venue will use an indoor court. The competition department is responsible for contacting the Shen Yuan Association to negotiate and borrow it. It is also heard that the work of the association is very intensive.

Educational News

Employment Training Class The Process of Enrolling Students Strictly Reviewed According to Standards from the 12th of This Month One Thousand Officially Admitted, Five Hundred on Waiting List, Two Batches of Equal Size to Be Enrolled

Graduates of vocational schools and above who have been recommended by various parties for the employment training class have exceeded the predetermined number of domestic and foreign graduates in the most recent three years. The standing committee members of the training class, in order to handle the matter carefully, held a meeting at the Executive Yuan to carefully formulate review standards and handed them over to the Ministry of Education of the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, the Central Political School, and the National Academic Work Advisory Office to send personnel to form a review committee to conduct the review. The committee, starting from the 12th of this month, began to strictly review all the academic records and certificates of the recommended students in accordance with the established standards. After going through the procedures of preliminary review and re-review, the review has been completed. A total of one thousand official students and five hundred waiting list students have been enrolled, with half of each enrolled in the first and second phases respectively. All official and waiting list students in each phase have been individually notified by the training class committee. At the same time, the physical examination and other procedures have also been decided. The official students in the first phase will undergo physical examinations at the Medical Education Committee of the Ministry of Education in Nanjing (inside the Ministry of Education) from October 1st to 3rd. (Members from remote provinces who have already been examined by the Education Department will not be re-examined.) Those who fail to arrive on time or fail the physical examination will be immediately removed from the list. The results of the physical examination and the start date of the school year, admission procedures, etc., will be notified to each student on October 5th. Those on the waiting list, upon receiving notification of replacement when there is a vacancy in the official list, should come to Beijing for a physical examination within the specified date. Those who fail to arrive on time will be disqualified for replacement. Furthermore, students enrolled in the second phase will be notified separately about their physical examination and other procedures to be completed before the start of the second phase (after the winter vacation). (Including those studying abroad) Those whose graduation qualifications have not yet been approved by the Ministry of Education should complete the relevant procedures in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Education before enrollment. There are other regulations for the order of replacement on the waiting list, which are not based on this list. The list of names will be announced in the advertisement column on the cover of today's newspaper. Also, (Among the 500 official students in the first phase, 467 are students from domestic schools in China, 9 are overseas students, and 24 are students from remote provinces. Among the 250 on the waiting list, 227 are from domestic schools in China, 13 are studying abroad, and 10 are from remote provinces. Among the 500 official students in the second phase, 486 are from domestic schools in China and 14 are from remote provinces. Among the 250 on the waiting list, all are students from domestic schools in China.

Cultivation of Youth and Guidance in Various Subjects

Order Issued by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education issued an order to the education bureaus of various counties, stating that youth students are the backbone of the country and society. In this extraordinary period, they must have the greatest preparation and effort to shoulder the important responsibility of saving the country and reviving the nation. Although there are many ways to prepare and make efforts, the most fundamental and essential is the cultivation of self-reliance. The way to cultivate self-reliance is, on the one hand, to cultivate character and establish a foundation for being a person, and on the other hand, to study knowledge in various subjects and enhance the power of service. Only with excellent character and rich scientific knowledge can one become a sound citizen and win the final victory in the national self-salvation struggle. However, young people have undetermined consciousness and little experience. Although they have the desire to work hard and improve, they still need active guidance to strengthen their will and expand their experience, so that they can use their efforts more economically and achieve greater results, and achieve the full success of self-reliance cultivation. The Department, in view of this, in addition to having formulated the "Methods for High School Students to Establish Aspirations" and issued it in Instruction No. 2584, has specially engaged experts to separately formulate the "Main Points for Guidance on Youth Cultivation" and the "Main Points for Guidance on the Study of Various Subjects for Middle School Students in Jiangsu Province," including Chinese, English, Mathematics, History and Geography, Physics, Chemistry, Biology, Art, and other subjects. In addition, there are also "Main Points for Guidance on General Studies," totaling ten types, which have been reviewed and completed by the Department separately, printed into a book, and ordered to be issued to various schools for implementation. When implementing the "Main Points for Guidance on the Study of Various Subjects," each school should refer to the research results of the relevant subjects of the Middle School Normal School Teaching Research Association. If there are any opinions, they should be reported separately before the end of the semester, so that they can be revised and supplemented in the future. In addition to separate orders, the above-mentioned "Main Points for Guidance on Cultivation and Study" in 10 types, totaling 0 books, are hereby issued, and the head of the bureau is ordered to comply and forward them to all secondary schools under its jurisdiction for compliance. This order.

New Offerings of Zhejiang University This Year

New Lineup of Department Heads and Professors

Equipment Fees Account for 26% of Expenses On the 14th of this month, Zhejiang University President Zhu, after performing the ritual at the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week, gave a report on the school's affairs, stating that the development of the school's affairs can be divided into two aspects: quality and quantity. In terms of quantity, the existing talent and equipment of Zhejiang University can accommodate 1,000 students. Considering the large number of freshmen applicants this year, the number of students should be increased in the future. However, school facilities must be increased and transformed. In terms of quality, regarding newly hired professors, there are Mei Guangdi, head of the Department of Foreign Languages ​​of the Faculty of Arts and Sciences, professors Lin Tianlan, Chen Xinheng, and the head of the Department of Education, which was originally concurrently held by Dean Zheng. This year, Zhuang Zexuan was invited to take over as head, Zhang Qiyun, head of the Department of History and Geography, professors Jing Changji and Zhu Tingyou, Zhang Shaozhong, head of the Department of Physics, professors Shu Xingbei, He Zenglu, and Wang Changgan, Zhang Zhaoxian, professor of the Department of Biology, Zhang Wenjun, head of the Department of Mechanical Engineering of the Faculty of Engineering, professors Zhou Chengyou, Qian Xiangbiao, and Hu Shusun, Wu Zhongwei, head of the Department of Civil Engineering, professors Liu Zhunye and Cheng Yaoxin of the Department of Chemical Engineering, and Dean of the Faculty of Agriculture Lu Shougeng. The College was originally divided into three departments and ten groups. This year, they were respectively merged into five departments: Agronomy, Horticulture, Sericulture, Plant Pathology and Entomology, and Agricultural Economics. The personnel are generally the same. New professors in the Department of Agronomy are Xu Tianxi and Sun Fengji, and Huang Benli. The head of the Department of Horticulture is Feng Yanan, and the professor of the Department of Sericulture is Zhang Zhenhua. The instrument fee for this year is 140,000 yuan. Together with the purchase of books, it amounts to 200,000 yuan, accounting for 26% of the school's total expenses, which is a large proportion among domestic universities. Except for the Faculty of Agriculture, the school buildings are all dilapidated, and places such as dormitories, sanatoriums, libraries, and physics rooms must be transformed. However, this year's budget has been established, and it is planned to propose a certain amount from temporary expenses for urgent construction. Starting from this academic year, it is stipulated that each student should have two extracurricular sports in addition to the regular physical education class, and actively advocate the development of sports habits for all teachers and students in the school. The Training Department has been newly established, with Director Jiang Zhenmin, and Sun Yachen and Chen Baiqing jointly presiding over it. It is also planned to invite deans, department heads, and professors to jointly bear the cost of training, in order to cultivate personality and return to goodness and beauty. In terms of publications, it is planned to publish a journal and organize an editorial department to take charge of it. The weekly magazine has recently been changed to a daily magazine, and news is transmitted faster. In addition, the five engineering societies donated 3,000 yuan as the school's "Engineering Scholarship Fund," with an annual interest of 300 yuan, to be given to students with excellent grades in the second grade of each department.

Personnel Management Association Holds Personnel Management Survey

Intensifying the Promotion of Personnel Management Work

Yesterday Held a Joint Meeting of Directors and Supervisors

Since the establishment of the Chinese Personnel Management Association, it has been nearly three years, and it has spared no effort in the research and improvement of personnel management work, and it has been deeply noticed and supported by all parties. It is learned that the Association held its 29th joint meeting of directors and supervisors at the Eight Immortals Bridge Youth Association yesterday, and also convened a regular meeting of the Anti-Corruption Committee at the same time. The attendees were He Qingru, Shen Jiucheng, Xiang Kangyuan, Gu Bingyuan, Zhang Yunbao, Pan Yangyao, Shi Jiuyun (on behalf of Gu), Zhang Yifan, Wen Chonglu, and Wu Zongwen. He Qingru chaired the meeting, and Wu Zongwen took the minutes. The reported matters were: 1. Chairman He reported on the recent state of the Association's affairs. The matters discussed were: (1) It was resolved that the Association, in order to intensify the promotion of personnel management work, will conduct surveys of the state of personnel management in various agencies in various regions, and regularly convene personnel management personnel in charge of various agencies for liaison; (2) It was resolved that the Personnel Management Monthly, in order to enrich its content, will be changed to a bimonthly publication, and the first issue of Volume 2 will be published on October 1st; (3) It was resolved that the Personnel Management Communication Research Institute will continue to be chaired by Director Tu Zheyin, and those interested in studying personnel management issues are welcome to register and join.

Shanghai World Bookstore Guanghua Harmonica is Excellent

The only completely domestic Guanghua brand harmonica made by the Shanghai Dahua Harmonica Company, with 21 and 23 holes, is exclusively sold by the Shanghai and various provincial and municipal World Bookstores. Its quality has been identified by Liu Yin, vice president and instructor of the China Harmonica Association, as having accurate, durable reeds, comparable to imported products priced at two or three yuan each, and even better than them. It is a credit to the Chinese craft industry, and the World Bookstore has always held a principle of small profits and high sales, setting the price at only 1.20 yuan per harmonica with 21 holes and 1.50 yuan per harmonica with 23 holes (add 20 cents for postage for mail orders). The goods are of high quality and the price is low. Recently, Chinese people have gradually become aware of this, so the sales of this harmonica have been very brisk recently, and many young people who love music across the country have one in hand.

After the opening, the price continued to decline due to persistent selling. HSBC's listing showed the UK and US both unchanged. There was a slight struggle in the middle, but the transaction was limited, and supply exceeded demand. The silver balance tax was revealed to have decreased by half a cent, continuing to decline slightly. Later, the market began to improve due to the joint submission of bars by large firms, gradually recovering. The trend was also stable at noon. The after-market opened slightly lower due to the supply of bars from Dingkang. After the opening, buyers jointly operated, gradually pulling up the price.
